Current Affairs Commentary: A Painful Word on the Fujian Rebellion 17

In the past, the brewing of political changes always began with verbal battles. After the exchange of letters and telegrams, they would then move to mediation. After a certain period of mediation, it would then begin to erupt. Today's Fujian rebellion, however, arose suddenly. Even if one wanted to mediate, it was too late. In the past, the launch of political changes was often limited to individuals and temporary issues of power. No matter how ambitious the warlords were, they still had to rely on the Three Principles of the People and never dared to abandon the Kuomintang's banner to establish their own. Today's Fujian rebellion, however, is using the slogan of withdrawing from the Kuomintang and establishing an all-people production government. Therefore, this change is of great significance. Several days ago, our port had already heard of this kind of rumor, but because we had not received reliable reports from Fujian, we did not dare to believe it deeply. Now, after reading the so-called Declaration of the Rights of the People of the People's Provisional Representative Assembly, its claims are relatively clear. The Central Government is the Central Government of the Kuomintang. From the perspective of the ruling party, this act of betraying the Party alone should already cause great anger and be severely punished without any hesitation. If the Fujian side still intends to proceed and has no intention of reining in at the brink of the precipice, then once the order to suppress the rebellion is implemented, another military disaster will inevitably arise. Here, we will temporarily set aside the goals and methods of this Fujian uprising and discuss the current situation of our country. We can no longer take any actions. Our country has suffered repeated disasters and successive wars in recent years. Moreover, banditry is rampant, rural areas are bankrupt, production is declining day by day, the unemployed population is increasing day by day, and the social economy is becoming increasingly unstable. The national situation has reached an extremely dangerous point. Moreover, it is exacerbated by the pressure of foreign aggression. Since the September 18th Incident last year, the people of the country have been calling for national salvation and resistance to foreign aggression every day, but the foreign aggression cannot be resisted and remains the same. Other issues, such as the autonomy of Inner Mongolia and the disturbances in Xinjiang, also have an impact on foreign affairs. As for the international situation, it has become increasingly tense recently. If another world war breaks out, and our country is involved, how can we protect ourselves? In this extremely dangerous situation, we can only hope that all parties will put aside their private opinions, abandon their concepts of power, and strive for unity, internally to reorganize politics and recuperate the people in order to survive, and externally to devote ourselves to transportation and develop border areas in order to consolidate national defense. In this way, there may still be a glimmer of hope for resurrection. Otherwise, it is like a doctor randomly prescribing medicine to a patient, not knowing how weak the patient's body is, and rashly prescribing a strong purgative. Even if the doctor does not necessarily lack the intention to cure the patient, what if the patient cannot withstand the medicine?

How much sympathy can Fujian's actions today win? How much danger does it put the country in? How much impact will it have on diplomacy? It is very strange that the leaders would do this rashly without careful consideration.

In yesterday's commentary "The Reefs of the Roosevelt Administration," the index of manufacturing production for July 1933 should be 101.0. This is hereby corrected.

President Chiang's Letter to All Officers and Soldiers of the 19th Route Army: "Hoping You Will Maintain Your Original Bandit Suppression Line, Not Be Swayed by Disordered Orders. Selfless Devotion to Righteousness Has Clear Historical Precedent, Rectifying Chaos and Returning to the Right is an Unshirkable Duty." 18

(Nanchang) President Chiang issued a letter to all officers and soldiers of the 19th Route Army, which stated: According to reports, Chen Mingshu, Li Jishen, and their ilk have seized Fuzhou, falsely using the name of our 19th Route Army, colluding with reactionary elements of the Third Party and the Social Democratic Party, advocating alliance with the Communists, betraying the Chinese Kuomintang, resisting the National Government, organizing their so-called Production Party, a guise for the Communist Party, and their so-called People's Revolutionary Government, abandoning the Party and national flag of the Blue Sky with a White Sun, created by our Party Leader since the revolution, and raising a rebel flag with a blue top, a red bottom, and five yellow stars embedded in the middle. At this time of serious national crisis, when the whole country is working together to suppress the Communists, they actually have this act of harming the Party and the country, hastening their own destruction. What is their intention? It is truly difficult to understand. The reason why Chen Mingshu and his like dare to brazenly launch this revolt is that they have actually reached a compromise with the Communist bandits in Jiangxi and Fujian, establishing a secret agreement of non-aggression, agreeing to provide supplies to the bandits, and planning military assistance and mutual support. This is evidenced by the presence of Huang Qixiang, Zhang Bojun, Peng Zexiang, and others, who are running errands for the Communist Party representatives, and the wife of Peng Dehuai remaining in Fuzhou, as well as the abolition of the national flag and Party emblem, and the high-sounding advocacy of land policies and worker-peasant policies. The claim of alliance with the Communists and betrayal of the Party is obvious. Furthermore, Chen Youren, who personally visited Shidehara the year before last to seek foreign assistance to occupy the Northeast, and Han Binli, who participated in the Nishihara Loan during the Anfu era, either hold new positions in the false government or act as envoys traveling east. Rumors abound, and the so-called conspiracy to sell out the country and harm the Party is credible. It is said that Chen and others are using the following as a pretext to spread their propaganda: on the one hand, they are threatening the officers and soldiers of our 19th Route Army, saying that if they do not ally with the Communist bandits in Fujian, they will be annihilated by the Communist bandits; on the other hand, they are deceiving the public with worker-peasant policies, implementing land revolution as a means of inciting them; and on the other hand, they are following the old trick of Fang Zhenwu and Ji Hongchang in North China, having already surrendered to Japan and colluded with the bandits, and then touting national salvation and resistance against Japan to deceive the officers and soldiers of our 19th Route Army. These traitors only use alliance with the Communists and collusion with Japan as a means, and destroying the Party and betraying the country as their goal. They have no regard for the glorious history of our 19th Route Army, and they do not care about the current fortunes and successes or failures of our 19th Route Army. The result will be that all the officers and soldiers of our 19th Route Army will be sacrificed and disgraced, which will not harm them in the slightest. Is this not a tragedy? Now, if we listen to the deception and manipulation of one or two people, and allow the entire Fujian to be lost to the Communist bandits, and are not allowed to sever ties with the Party and the country, and are scolded by both domestic and foreign observers, I fear that if the martyrs of our 19th Route Army, who sacrificed themselves for the suppression of the Communists and resistance against Japan, were to know, they would surely weep bitterly in the afterlife. Alas, my loyal and courageous officers and soldiers of the 19th Route Army! You once gained a good reputation for suppressing the Communists, resisting Japan, and not participating in internal wars. Now, you are being held hostage by the rebel Chen, and have become the ringleaders in destroying the Party and the country. What will you say to defend yourselves before the people of the country? How will you face the spirit of the Party Leader in heaven? How will you meet the martyrs who suppressed the Communists and resisted Japan in the afterlife? Should it not be the case that you, the officers and soldiers of my 19th Route Army, have followed me, Zhongzheng, in expeditions east and battles north, sharing life and death and hardships for more than a hundred battles since the thirteenth year of the Republic? You have established great achievements in the revolutionary process, and your heroic deeds are recorded in history. You are truly a loyal, courageous, and fighting army of the Party and the country. How can you be the private property of Chen Mingshu and his ilk? At this time of crisis and shock, you must be able to stand on your own with the spirit of loving the country and protecting the people, and you must not harm the public for private gain, or allow yourselves to be sacrificed for any individual's rebellion against the Party and the country. In particular, you should not blindly follow and echo the changes of heart of one or two people, and allow the merits and glory you have earned in the past, risking life and limb, to be destroyed. My loyal and courageous officers and soldiers, you understand the greater good and must have weighed things carefully. There is no need for further words. At this moment, the central authorities recognize that the only urgent task and the only way out for the country is to strive to suppress the Red bandits, which is the only way to defend the Party and the country and save it from danger. In recent days, the military operations to suppress the bandits in Jiangxi have made rapid progress. I, Zhongzheng, continue to order our bandit suppression forces to focus on completing the work of bandit suppression. I will never allow the Fujian Incident to affect the military operations of bandit suppression, nor will I allow the troops who have shared hardships for ten years to be deceived by one or two unscrupulous people, causing our national revolution to kill each other, leading to the shaking of the bandit suppression front, and fulfilling the Communist bandits' pre-determined plot to instigate the Fujian Incident in order to shatter our five encirclement and suppression plans, and also giving our enemies a chance to laugh at us. As for the ringleaders of the Fujian Incident, we will observe their future actions and give them a chance to become aware and reform themselves. I hope that the officers and soldiers of my 19th Route Army will all understand this intention, on the one hand, maintaining your original bandit suppression line and not being swayed by disordered orders, and on the other hand, striving to clarify justice and promote repentance from the rebellion. Selfless devotion to righteousness has clear historical precedent, and rectifying chaos and returning to the right is an unshrinkable duty. Saving the country and saving yourselves, the key lies here. I hope that my officers and soldiers will quickly consider this and act accordingly. I have high hopes for you. Chiang Chung-cheng, November 22nd. (Central News Agency telegram, 22nd)

Talk by Yang Xiaocang, Military Attache at the Embassy in Japan 24

(Nanjing) Yang Xiaocang, military attache at the embassy in Japan, returned to China. After visiting Chiang in Jiangxi, he came to Nanjing. According to him, recently the Soviet Russia proposed to Japan to conclude a non-aggression treaty. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs also agreed, but it was opposed by a part of the military, and it could not be concluded in the end. Afterwards, the situation between the two sides gradually deteriorated, but the Russian side still intends to find ways to ease it. Judging from the fact that the Russian government sold the Chinese Eastern Railway, which it had no right to sell this year, to Japan, its desire to ease the conflict between Japan and Russia is very obvious, but it has also failed to become a reality. Until now, the situation between the two sides has become tense, but according to my personal observation, it will not lead to a break. Modern warfare is not comparable to what it was ten years ago. If it does not start, then it is over. Once it breaks out, then green gas and poisonous gas will all appear on the battlefield, and huge constructions and most of humanity can be destroyed in an instant. Since the European War, the world's countries have not recovered their vitality, and countries have not failed to advocate peace, but the hearts of mutual suspicion have not diminished slightly. They verbally say to reduce armaments, but secretly they are actively enriching them. In short, current events are unexpected. Sometimes a country or two may cause a second world war due to trivial matters, which is unknown. Domestic political views in Japan are extremely diverse, but the power faction is more powerful. The people are all very patriotic. As for the economic situation, under the world's economic depression, the country is becoming more and more difficult, but whether the management is appropriate or not, it is because having money cannot be controlled, and it is better for those who have no money to have a calculation. Since the 918 Incident, many overseas Chinese in Japan have returned to China. In total, there are about several thousand overseas Chinese now, but they are all very poor and there are many unemployed. In the past, most of the overseas Chinese in Japan sold Japanese goods. After the 918 Incident, they all refused to sell Japanese goods, and their ambition is commendable. Therefore, the Japanese have also taken back self-operation and no longer rely on our overseas Chinese. Therefore, overseas Chinese are unemployed and extremely poor, and they should be provided with relief. I returned to China this time due to illness and will take a short-term rest. The date of return to office is undecided. (Special telegram, 22nd)

Guangdong Provincial Economic Conference Opens. The Authorities Plan to Borrow 10 Million Yuan to Maintain Paper Currency 26

(Hong Kong) The Guangdong Provincial Economic Conference opened on the 22nd. (Special telegram, 22nd)

The United States and Russia End All Outstanding Issues. Russia Owes the United States 768.5 Million Yuan in Old Debts. The United States Compensates Russia 15 Million Yuan for Damage from Military Intervention. The New Agreement Can Be Established Today 27

(Washington) It is heard that the United States and Russia will be able to establish a new agreement on Thursday, ending all previous entanglements and starting a new relationship. This agreement is currently being negotiated between Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov and officials from the US State Department and the Treasury Department. After it is compiled, it can completely resolve the old Russian debts to the US and the US overseas Chinese's requests for confiscated property, and the Soviet Russian requests for the military intervention in Archangel, etc. The Russian debt to the United States has been a major obstacle to the resumption of diplomatic relations for sixteen years, totaling about 768,500,000 yuan in principal and interest, of which the principal includes 86,000,000 yuan of public bonds issued by Imperial Russia in the United States, 187,000,000 yuan borrowed by the Kerensky government in the United States, 111,000,000 yuan of Imperial Russian war debts in the hands of Americans, and 60,500,000 yuan of property confiscated by Soviet Russia. The reason for Soviet Russia's refusal to pay is that it considers this public debt to have been used by the previous government to suppress the working class. The fettered people should not be held responsible for paying the value of the fetters, and the Communist Party had fully warned that it would not recognize this debt, and Germany denied previous debts after the revolution, citing the example of the US federal government refusing to repay 300 million yuan in debt. As for the Soviet Russia's request for compensation for damages from the Allied intervention in Siberia and northern Russia, it once requested 60,000,000,000 yuan, of which the United States should bear a certain amount, which has never been divided. Now, according to the exchange of documents, Soviet Russia has abandoned its claim for damages for the Siberian part, and only claims the Archangel part. The legal basis for this Soviet Russian claim is the previous American Alabama case, which made the British compensate 15 million yuan as a precedent. Currently, Litvinov and US Ambassador to Russia Bullitt, Undersecretary of State Ferry, Burr, and Acting Secretary of the Treasury Morganthau have been consulting for days to discuss solutions. Litvinov is scheduled to go to New York for a welcome banquet on Thursday afternoon and return home by boat on Saturday, but if necessary, it may be postponed to ensure that the negotiations in the United States are completely concluded before returning. (National Telegram, 21st)

Disarmament Adjournment Issue, Direct Conflict Between France and Italy, Britain Supports Italy, United States Indifferent 30

(Geneva) It is heard tonight that France and Italy have failed to agree on the question of whether the Commission on the Control of Armaments should adjourn, and the plan for a two-month adjournment of the Disarmament Conference may be affected. It is reported that if a compromise cannot be found before tomorrow, the Steering Committee may not recommend adjournment. Currently, the French representative, Paul-Boncour, is striving to ensure that the Commission on the Control of Armaments continues to meet during the disarmament adjournment period; otherwise, the French representative will insist that the General Commission should still convene on December 4th as originally planned. The Italian representative, De Suàlogna, stated that without German participation, technical work would be futile and inappropriate, and that if the Commission on the Control of Armaments continues to meet, Italy will no longer participate. The British attitude is moderately in favor of the Italian position, while the United States seems largely indifferent. After a day of heated debate between the two sides, Chairman Henderson was authorized to recommend to the Steering Committee tomorrow that the question of whether the Commission on the Control of Armaments should adjourn be left to Henderson and others to decide. However, Paul-Boncour stated that he understands this to mean that the Commission on the Control of Armaments should continue to work, while the Italian representative stated that it should be understood as a suspension of work. Therefore, it is expected that the debate in tomorrow's Steering Committee meeting will be more intense than anything seen since the opening of the Disarmament Conference. (National Telegram, 21st)

(Geneva) The disarmament talks have created a new crisis because of France's insistence that the Technical Committee should continue its work during the adjournment of the Disarmament Conference. French Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour insisted that work must continue, but representatives from Britain, Italy, and the United States did not agree. The Italian representative said that some problems might cause unexpected dangers. After four hours of discussion, today's meeting broke up without results. The issue will be discussed in tomorrow's Disarmament Conference Steering Committee meeting. It is understood that French representative Paul-Boncour intends to convene the General Commission if he cannot achieve his goal, as he considers this a matter of principle. (Reuters, 21st)

(London) This afternoon, Prime Minister MacDonald reported to the House of Commons on the progress of the Geneva disarmament talks, saying that Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference has created a new situation. It is now necessary to consider the problems themselves and reach a compromise before the Disarmament Conference can continue. The Disarmament Conference has never retreated, and it has never been a question of advancing or retreating. What is doubtful now is only what is the best procedure at present. In recent days, Simon and Eden have held beneficial and moderate talks with Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson and representatives from various countries. Simon returned to Beijing this morning. It is said that Geneva has a very good and firm spirit of cooperation, and does not want the disarmament work to end in failure or stagnation. Simon's trip to Geneva was on behalf of the entire British Cabinet, so it can be said that the British government's joint efforts necessary for the final victory have been very laborious. We hope that Germany can join this kind of diplomatic exchange of views, and hope to continue its efforts so that the Disarmament Conference can achieve good results. As for the United Kingdom, it has always been tireless in this matter. We, of course, should still be in close contact with the United States on all events. The Prime Minister continued,

There are many floating rumors about the work of the British so-called munitions factories, which is regrettable. Sheffield factories currently have no foreign orders for munitions. Roosevelt's Monetary Policy, Rise of Opponents, Resignation of Treasury Advisor Approved 44

(Washington) Sprague, the Chief Advisor of the U.S. Treasury Department and one of the world's leading monetary experts, who once served as an advisor to the Bank of England, resigned from his post today due to disagreement with the U.S. government's monetary policy, stating that he will help create public opinion against Roosevelt's plan, believing that at present, there is no way to prevent the dangerous path of unlimited inflation except by arousing public opinion. Therefore, he is severing his relationship with the government. He also said that the current policy may completely bankrupt the government's credit, because the Treasury's expenditures far exceed its revenues. It is expected that between now and the end of the fiscal year, it will be necessary to borrow 200 million yuan to make up for the losses of the government's various new experiments. He also strongly attacked the gold purchase plan in his letter, saying that he believes that purchasing gold abroad cannot raise prices, because since the price decline in the current environment, it has not been able to promote the need for materials or labor. To raise world prices, there must be a situation sufficient to increase the need for labor and materials, and then production and services can be increased, and living standards can also be improved. Sprague also said that when the government is determined to depress the gold yuan, public debt becomes an unsatisfactory investment, especially government public debt, so most government public debt is currently below face value. He believes that if the President does not abandon the current monetary policy in the future, he will inevitably resort to issuing more banknotes to meet government expenditures. (National Telegram, 21st)

Warm Springs President Roosevelt has approved Professor Sprague's resignation without saying a word. President Roosevelt's secretary told people that President Roosevelt's monetary program will not be affected by Professor Sprague's resignation. (Reuters, 21st)

(Washington) President Roosevelt today formed an executive committee for the purpose of standardizing the government's commercial policy in order to centralize the government's control over import and export trade. Undersecretary of State Phillips has been appointed as chairman of the committee. All matters relating to foreign trade and the negotiation of commercial treaties will be consulted with the committee. (Reuters, 21st)

Newspapers have commented on Professor Sprague's resignation, praising his loyalty and courage. The New York Times said that Professor Sprague's letter to President Roosevelt should not be described as clumsy or malicious. Takahashi Announces, Domestic Gold Purchase Policy, Price Based on London Gold Price 45

India Approves International Silver Agreement; Silver Sales Restricted from January Next Year 46

The Indian Parliament in New Delhi today approved the International Silver Agreement. The Finance Member of the Viceroy's Executive Council, Sir George Schuster, welcomed the agreement, regarding it as an achievement of international cooperation. He stated that a mere rise in the price of silver would not increase India's purchasing power. However, the situation is different for China, whose currency is based on silver. A high silver price increases China's purchasing power, but this is only temporary, as a high exchange rate only temporarily encourages imports. The Silver Agreement was signed in London at the close of the World Economic Conference by silver-using countries India, China, and Spain, and silver-producing countries Canada, Mexico, the United States, Australia, and Peru. This agreement restricts the Indian government from selling silver. Starting from January of next year, silver sales should not exceed 140 million ounces within four years, averaging 35 million ounces per year. If silver sales in any year are less than this amount, the remainder should be added to the amount to be sold in the following year, but no more than 50 million ounces can be sold in one year. The Indian government has the right to sell silver to countries willing to pay off American war debts with silver. If this agreement leads to India selling 175 million ounces of silver at any point during these four years, the agreement will be automatically terminated. China undertakes not to sell or destroy silver obtained from circulating currency during these four years. At the same time, Canada, the United States, Australia, Mexico, and Peru all undertake not to sell silver during these four years and to purchase or recover 35 million ounces of mined silver from the silver market each year. The distribution of this amount will be negotiated by the governments of the countries concerned. This agreement must be ratified by the governments of the countries concerned before April 1, 1934. (Reuter, 21st)

American Prisoners Riot; Police Open Fire with Machine Guns to Suppress Uprising 47

At the Eastern State Penitentiary in Philadelphia, USA, today, 1,300 prisoners rioted in the prison yard during gymnastics. Five hundred police officers, machine gunners, and firefighters were quickly dispatched to suppress the uprising, which was eventually quelled. During gymnastics today, upon a prearranged signal, 73 prisoners rushed out to the textile room, setting it on fire and destroying machinery. The remaining prisoners burned bedding in the prison. By the time the firefighters arrived, the fire had spread to the kitchen and laundry room. To prevent prisoners from escaping, machine guns were mounted on the walls around the prison. Later, the police opened fire with machine guns, forcing the prisoners back to their cells. The situation has now been restored to order. (Reuter, 21st)

Xi'an Daily President Qiu Yuanwu Assassinated; Wang Sends Telegram to Yang and Shao to Strictly Arrest the Murderer 59

(Xi'an) Qiu Yuanwu, the president of the Xi'an Daily, came here in March of this year to found the newspaper at the order of the central government. For nine months, he has worked diligently and spared no effort. He was repeatedly threatened by reactionary elements out of jealousy. Qiu dedicated himself to the country and continued to fight with a spirit of fearlessness, not slacking off in the slightest. On the evening of the 21st, he went to a friend's appointment in Xiaochejia Lane. At about 7 pm, he returned to the newspaper office to work. As soon as he stepped out of the door, he was met by five or six thugs armed with pistols and sharp knives who attacked him head-on. More than ten shots were fired. Qiu suffered two gunshot wounds and two knife wounds, one gunshot wound and one knife wound to the head, one knife wound to the chest, and one gunshot wound to the abdomen. He died on the spot. The local press was shocked by the news and decided to hold a meeting to petition the authorities to strictly arrest the murderers and provide practical protection to the press. Qiu was 26 years old, from Quanjiao, Anhui, and graduated from Sun Yat-sen College. He served successively in the Qingdao Special City Party Committee, the Inner Mongolia Party Affairs Steering Committee, and the Anhui and Hubei Provincial Party Committees. He achieved outstanding results in handling party affairs and was deeply praised by the central government. Now, he has suffered an unexpected tragedy. He leaves behind an elderly mother, a wife, and two sons, one five years old and the other only three years old. His situation after death is desolate and deeply tragic. (Central News Agency, 21st)

(Nanjing) Qiu Yuanwu, the president of the Xi'an Daily, was shot and killed by reactionary elements at 7 pm on the 21st. President Wang was extremely shocked upon hearing the news. On the 22nd, he sent a special telegram to Director Yang Hucheng and Chairman Shao Lizi, ordering them to strictly arrest the murderers and bring them to justice, and to protect the comrades of the Xi'an Daily. The original telegram read: To Director Yang Hucheng and Chairman Shao Lizi of Xi'an, I am deeply shocked to learn that Comrade Qiu Yuanwu, the president of the Xi'an Daily, was shot and killed by reactionary elements yesterday. I hope that you will immediately order the arrest of the murderer and punish him according to the law. I also hope that you will protect the comrades of the Xi'an Daily. Shanhaiguan to be Fully Received by the End of the Month; Tao Shangming and Others Accompany Chaishan to Shanhaiguan; Japanese Troops at Various Ports Can be Fully Withdrawn After February; Establishment of Customs is Under Investigation 81

A Beiping dispatch states that Shanhaiguan is scheduled to be received within days. Huang He sent Tao Shangming and Zhu Shiqin as representatives to Shanhaiguan along with Yin Shousong, the magistrate of Linyu County, to negotiate the receipt procedures. Tao and others went to Tianjin the night before to contact the Hebei Provincial Government and visit Nakamura, the commander of the Japanese Tianjin Garrison. It was decided that tomorrow night (22nd) they will go to Shanhaiguan. Chaishan, a military attache from the Japanese Embassy, will accompany them. It is expected that they will arrive in Shanhaiguan at 7:00 am on the 23rd, and after negotiating the receipt procedures with Endo, the staff officer of the 14th Mixed Brigade of the Japanese Army, and Ochiai, the commander of the Shanhaiguan garrison, the receipt will begin on the 25th and can be completed by the end of this month. The 14th Mixed Brigade of the Japanese Army, in addition to the original garrison, has mostly withdrawn to Jinzhou. Currently, only about two hundred troops remain stationed. After the defense is handed over, all troops can be fully withdrawn. Whether the organs of the puppet state and the local maintenance association will be completely abolished or moved outside the Guan are yet to be determined. According to the Japanese, the Japanese barracks outside the Guan can be completed within two months. The Japanese troops currently stationed at various passes of the Great Wall can be fully withdrawn two months later, and the receipt of the various passes can also be carried out successively. However, the puppet troops stationed at Malan Village, citing the protection of the mausoleum, have not yet withdrawn. After negotiations between our side and the Japanese side, they finally agreed to withdraw.

The establishment of customs at various passes is currently under investigation to ascertain the actual situation at each pass. Zhang Yongnian, the deputy commissioner of taxation, has returned from a survey of Gubeikou and will go to survey Xifengkou, Jieling, and Lengkou tomorrow. The puppet government has set up checkpoints at Shanhaiguan and Gubeikou to levy taxes. The locations of the customs are all inside the Guan. The establishment of customs at Xifengkou and Lengkou is also in preparation. Whether the puppet government's checkpoints can be moved outside the Guan in the future is still a problem. If our side establishes customs at the same location where the puppet government has already established customs in the future, disputes are inevitable, which is a real question. If it is located farther away, it will be easier to steal and evade duties for goods entering the Guan. Currently, most of the goods coming and going are groceries going out and contraband coming in. The Japanese have established long-distance bus companies at various key points, specializing in transporting these contraband items, so that our side cannot carry out inspections effectively. This is also a major problem in the future. Therefore, even if we establish customs, if the Japanese rely on strong power and do not accept inspections, all contraband items cannot be banned, and all goods cannot be effectively taxed, then each pass is tantamount to being established in vain. (November 21)

North China After the Fujian Incident: Central Government Cables Emphasize Prevention of a Third Party; He Yingqin Convenes Meeting of Generals 82

Beiping Dispatch: With Chen Mingshu and others' unusual moves in Fujian and their establishment of a separate banner, the Central Government is sincerely worried that disgruntled military personnel and politicians in North China might seize the opportunity to secretly incite unrest. Those present included Yu Xuezhong, Wan Fulin, Shang Zhen, He Zhuguo, Pang Bingxun, Wang Shuchang, Gao Guizi, Shen Ke, Bao Wenye, Jiang Bocheng, Wang Yizhe, Guan Linzheng, Huang Jie, and over ten others. He also stated that during this time of national crisis, the sudden incident in Fujian was particularly unfortunate. The situation in North China has not yet passed the danger point, and he hoped that the generals would appreciate the Central Government's intentions and work together to maintain the precarious situation. The generals also expressed their sincere unity and willingness to face the national crisis together. Finally, it was decided to separately order their subordinates to strictly guard against the activities of the Third Party in various parts of North China in order to maintain治安and stabilize people's hearts. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 p.m. In the afternoon, He issued another circular, ordering the Chairman of the Provincial Government, Yu Xuezhong, to rush back to Tianjin tomorrow night to make arrangements. Song Zheyuan, who was recuperating in Tianjin, was also summoned by telegram to come to Beiping around 11:00 p.m. tonight and will soon return to Chahar to take charge. The Fujian Situation Tenses: Zhang Qun Summoned to Nanjing to Discuss Major Plans to Address the Situation; Zhang Expresses Opinions on the Fujian Incident 83

Hankou Dispatch: The independence of Li Jishen, Chen Mingshu, and others in Fujian has changed from rumors to reality. In order to deal with this serious situation, Premier of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei telegraphed Zhang Qun, member of the Central Committee and Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, on the 21st, summoning him to Nanjing to discuss major plans. On the same day, former Director of the Aviation Administration Huang Bingheng arrived in Hankou from Nanjing to visit Zhang. That evening at 9:00 p.m., they boarded the Taikoo Company's Wusong Wheel eastward. Due to the hasty departure, Zhang was accompanied only by his secretary, Feng Fei. Provincial government affairs were temporarily entrusted to Lu Zhu, member of the Provincial Committee and Secretary-General, to handle on his behalf. Before his departure, Zhang made a statement to reporters, saying, "The unusual situation in Fujian, I do not yet know the truth. I have just received a telegram from Premier Wang, asking me to discuss major plans to deal with the Fujian situation, so I am leaving immediately. I will be able to get detailed information after arriving in Nanjing. At this time of domestic and foreign troubles, the whole country should unite sincerely, consolidate the central government, and save the country from danger. How can there be further division? Today's events are truly heartbreaking. After completing my official business in Nanjing, I will go to Shanghai and then return to Nanchang to visit Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. I can return to Hubei in about two weeks. This visit to Chiang Kai-shek will be to report on two matters: (1) the resettlement of migrants in the recovered bandit areas of the Henan-Hubei-Anhui border region; (2) the joint issuance of silver dollar notes by the Hubei Provincial Bank and the Four Provinces Farmers Bank. Regarding the resettlement issue, when Commander-in-Chief Liu Zhenhua passed through Hankou a few days ago, he discussed it in detail with me, Director He, and Chief of Staff Cao. Commander-in-Chief Liu advocated that the people in the bandit areas should be completely moved out and arrangements should be made for their resettlement, with the expenses borne by the Provincial Government. The expenses for the armed people who moved into the bandit areas will be borne by the Border Area Bandit Suppression Headquarters. I believe that the people of our country have a deep sense of homeland and are unwilling to leave their homeland and move to a foreign land. Therefore, the resettlement of the people who are moved out is really a difficult task. In order to avoid this difficulty, it is best to choose a wasteland near the bandit area and move them there. This not only meets their attachment to their homeland, but also achieves the practical effect of resettling migrants and eliminating bandits. In the future, when the remaining bandits are defeated, it will be more convenient to return to their hometowns. Commander-in-Chief Liu expressed his great approval of this plan. In addition to Commander-in-Chief Liu going to Nanchang to report to Chiang Kai-shek first, I will also make a presentation and ask for approval for implementation. Regarding the joint issuance of silver dollar notes by the two banks, all the measures have been completely decided, and the two banks will jointly organize a public treasury. The candidate for the head of the treasury has also been internally determined (said to be former Director of Finance Shen Zhaonian). After the establishment of the public treasury, silver dollar notes will be issued, and the reserve will be kept by the public treasury to ensure that they can be cashed at any time. This matter will also be reported in detail to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek when I go to Jiangxi," and so on.

Provincial Chairman Zhang Qun previously received a telegram from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, ordering him to draft measures to reverse the declining trends in the counties of southern Hubei, where the local customs are lazy and particularly fond of gambling. After receiving the order, Zhang immediately ordered the Civil Affairs, Construction, and Education Departments to jointly draft measures and submit them for approval. On the 21st, they had drafted and submitted them to the Provincial Government. The measures are divided into two parts: active and passive. Active aspects: (1) Revitalize the rural economy: 1. Establish branches of the Four Provinces Farmers Bank; 2. Organize credit cooperatives in various counties; 3. Promote the warehouse system; (2) Develop transportation and develop industries; (3) Education: 1. School education; 2. Compulsory education; 3. Social education; (4) Resettle refugees and grant them land for cultivation; (5) Improve customs and promote thrift. Passive aspects: (1) Eliminate idleness; (2) Strictly prohibit opium and gambling. (November 21st)

The Pseudo 15th Army Corps Suffers a Disastrous Defeat in Attacking Daxiongguan; Over a Thousand Bandits Killed, and Twice as Many Wounded; Li and Guo Divisions Achieve Miraculous Feats 84

Nanchang Dispatch: On the 12th of this month, the pseudo 7th Army Corps penetrated into Xuwan, dozens of miles away from Fu, and planned to ambush the pseudo 3rd Army Corps in the Maodian area, attempting to attack Fuzhou. Fortunately, the Xing Division took a roundabout route from Langju to aid Xu, joining forces with the 36th Division to completely defeat the pseudo 37th Army Corps. The bandits then retreated to the Xiaoshi area. Unexpectedly, they again used the pseudo 1st and 5th Army Corps to attack Yihuang. Fortunately, the Li Yannian and Guo Siyan Divisions of the National Army stationed in Yihuang advanced from Tangyin to Yongxing Quanshi. The bandits in that area fled south to Dangkou. On the 19th, the Zhu bandits suddenly launched an attack on Daxiongguan (between Yongxing Bridge and Rao, south of Yihuang) from Shagang Shangdangkou, and the Shengang areas by Lin Biao's pseudo 1st, 2nd, and 3rd Divisions and Dong Zhentang's 13th, 14th, and 15th Divisions, with great ferocity. At the same time, small groups harassed Xianfang between Yihuang and Fuzhou in an attempt to cut off the National Army's transportation. At that time, the Li Division firmly defended its original position, relying on fortifications to strike the bandits head-on with intensive charges. After several hours of bloody battle, they finally defeated the bandits. At about 1:00 p.m. on the 20th, the General Headquarters received a phone call from Fuzhou stating, "The pseudo 15th Army Corps attacking the Li Division's position at Daxiongguan was completely repulsed by us, killing over a thousand bandits and wounding twice as many. We captured 29 machine guns and 1,500 rifles. The remaining bandits are retreating south and are being pursued." Further news from Fuzhou stated that the pseudo 37th Army Corps, which had previously attacked Xuwan from Jinxi, was still lingering around Zixi Jinxi, and from time to time raided near Xuwan from Langju Zuofangying, but were all defeated by the local defense forces. According to captured bandit soldiers in Xuwan, the 19th and 20th Divisions, which attacked Xu, were Fang Shaobu's elite troops and lost most of their strength. The pseudo 4th, 5th, and 6th Divisions, which fought a bloody battle with the National Army's 4th Division at Fengshanpu, were Peng Dehuai's main force and were also almost completely wiped out. From this, it can be seen that there are hardly any remnants of the bandits left. (November 20th)

Bandit Wu Qingxiang of Songjiang Escorted to the Provincial Capital 85

The bandit Wu Qingxiang, a major criminal who robbed the family of Fan Bingnan, a villager in Panshe Township, District 16, was arrested. After interrogation by the county government, the facts were clear. Due to the seriousness of the case, the county government sent Police Chief Dong Futang and others in vehicle number 36 yesterday to escort him to the Zhenjiang Provincial Security Department for trial.

The Verification of an Old Woman in Suzhou Strangling Her Prodigal Son 86

The old woman Fei Fan, from Miaojiaoshang Village, at the foot of Mount Shizi in the Mudu District of Suzhou, owned hundreds of acres of good land. She had three sons: the eldest named Laohu (Tiger), the second Asi (Four), and the youngest Genhu (Root Tiger). They had all married and lived separately. Asi lived with his mother, his wife Qiu, his son Tugen, and his daughter-in-law in the old house. Laohu and Genhu lived separately and were both hardworking, thrifty, and law-abiding. However, Asi developed a habit of smoking opium more than ten years ago, did not engage in production, and sold off his land year by year. Recently, as he became more impoverished, his behavior became even worse, earning him the disdain of the entire village. Fortunately, his mother, wife, son, and daughter-in-law were still able to support themselves. Recently, Asi asked his mother for money for opium, and when he was refused, he often beat and abused her. On the 13th of this month, news suddenly came that Asi had hanged himself. The court approved an exemption from autopsy. Afterwards, it was widely rumored that Asi had been strangled to death by his mother, and that his wife Qiu and his brother Genhu were involved. Therefore, the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau arrested Fei Fan, Fei Qiu, and the local guarantor Li Songting and sent them to the local court in the city. Yesterday (22nd), prosecutor Lu Wenqin, clerk Xuan Fang, and forensic doctor Mao Yaoting were sent by the local prosecutor's office to the village for an autopsy. Since the body had already been buried, they immediately exhumed the grave and opened the coffin. Upon examination, it was found that the skin of Asi's corpse was very white, which was inconsistent with the redness of the skin of a person who had hanged himself and whose blood had settled. There was a very obvious rope mark on the back of his neck, and there was blood in his mouth and nose. There were injuries on his hands, feet, and face. It was clear that he had been strangled to death. After filling out the coroner's report, they summoned the deceased's son, Tugen, for questioning. According to his statement, his father's behavior was usually absurd, and his grandmother was dissatisfied with him. He did not know why he died because he was at his wife's home at the time. The judge also investigated the villagers and learned that the deceased's wife, Qiu, usually treated her mother-in-law with great filial piety. Whether she colluded with her aunt to strangle her husband is still under investigation. The deceased's brother, Genhu, was also afraid of being implicated and had already fled without a trace. The judge immediately returned to the city to report the information for further investigation.

Judgment in an Ancestor-Descendant Property Dispute Case 87

Zhou Zhenyi, the adopted son of the deceased wealthy merchant Zhou Nianqin of Yinma Bridge, Hulong Street, sued his grandmother, Xu, for failing to hand over the inheritance of 400,000 yuan in cash, 3,000 mu of fields, and 19 houses left by his deceased father, which had been managed by his grandmother, Xu. He claimed that he had now started a family and was entitled to inherit the estate. He had repeatedly asked his grandmother to hand it over, but she had refused. Therefore, he filed a lawsuit in court. Yesterday (22nd), the court ruled that the defendant should pay the plaintiff one-half of Zhou Nianqin's estate, totaling 650 mu of fields and 17 houses, as well as 3,000 silver dollars.

Resolution of the Wuxi Garment Industry Labor Dispute 88

The labor dispute in the local garment industry has been brewing for several days and has not yet been resolved. County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, in order to mediate, convened representatives of the silk and satin industry's "new outfit" department to the county on the 21st of this month, together with the Party Headquarters and the Chamber of Commerce, for talks. As a result, two principles of mediation were decided: (1) The silk and satin industry's "new outfit" department shall not create gift items and other pretexts to solicit business by improper means; (2) The price of Chinese garments should be in accordance with the general standards of the garment industry and should not be deliberately suppressed. At the same time, County Magistrate Yan convened a second meeting with the industry and said that although the current garment industry dispute was ostensibly caused by the "new outfit" department, the root cause was actually the unfair competition within the silk and satin industry. The dispute between the garment industry and the "new outfit" department has been resolved by the government and the Party Headquarters together. However, the silk and satin industry is engaging in open and secret struggles, vying with each other to offer gifts and price reductions, which may lead to disputes at any time. It has now been decided that all silk and satin shops should cancel all items such as extra sizes, price reductions, and gifts by the end of this month. From December onwards, the guild should discuss and formulate uniform measures and formulate disciplinary measures for those who violate industry regulations, and report them to the Party and government organs for record, in order to permanently eliminate disputes. The representatives of the silk industry who attended the meeting unanimously agreed. As for the garment industry guild, because this labor dispute has been fairly mediated by the Party and government authorities, a stage has been reached. Yesterday, it specially notified all members to resume work from today.

Nantong Five Mountains Daily News Sealed Up 89

The Five Mountains Daily News in Nantong was founded by Qian Xiaowu, a local resident. Since its publication on February 1, 1933, it has been fair in its arguments and has enjoyed a great reputation. Recently, because it published news that the Tiandetang Clothing Store was fined heavily for selling enemy goods, it was sealed up by the County Party Headquarters on the morning of the 18th. At present, Qian Xiaowu, the general manager and editor-in-chief of the newspaper, arrived in Shanghai yesterday and will soon go to the province to appeal to all parties in the Party and government, and plans to report the situation to the Journalists Association of this city and request assistance, and is currently contacting them separately.

Announcement of the Verdict in the Wu Junyu Embezzlement Case 93

In the case of Wu Junyu, the former Director of the Construction Bureau of Kunshan County, embezzling public funds, the Zhenjiang Court announced its verdict yesterday. Wu Junyu was sentenced to three years and eight months of imprisonment for the joint and continuous embezzlement of items held in public office, and deprived of his civil rights for eight years. In addition, Wu Junyu should compensate the plaintiff in the incidental civil lawsuit, the Construction Bureau, with 127,316 yuan, six jiao, two fen, and two li of public funds. It is reported that Wu expressed his dissatisfaction and plans to hire a lawyer to draft an appeal.

The Director of the Yangzhou Business Tax Bureau Arrested for Malpractice 94

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, according to investigator Zhou Zhengyuan, found that the business tax payments for the summer and autumn seasons of this year paid by the three pharmacies Peng Taihe, Dade Sheng, and Tongsong, and the Tianfu general merchandise store in Yangzhou, did not match the reports on the review reports of the county business bureau. Moreover, the tax payments paid by each industry each quarter were mostly ratified by the guild of the same industry and apportioned by store, without receipts. The Department believed that the Business Tax Bureau had engaged in corruption and had enriched itself, and immediately dismissed Li Mingqian, the Director of the 6th District and Bureau. It also secretly telegraphed County Magistrate Ma to have Li placed under surveillance and await investigation. On the evening of the 20th, the county sent the Chief Inspector of Public Security to lead the police to Li's private residence, where Li was arrested and detained at the Bureau to await the Department's handling. As for the successor, Song Shenzhi has been appointed by the Department to take over.

Major Fire Outside the East Gate of Qingjiang 95

Outside the East Gate of Huaiyin, the most lively area, apart from Huajie, is the Wenmiao Street. Therefore, the residents' houses there are closely arranged and densely populated. Yesterday, at 3:00 p.m., a careless accident occurred in the home of Fan Yucheng, a water carrier in Hejia Lane, that place. Since both Fan Yucheng and his wife were not at home, the fire spread greatly, extending to the houses of neighboring residents downwind. For a time, the flames filled the sky and could not be contained. Dozens of water dragons, both Chinese and foreign, went to the scene to fight the fire and demolished the houses connected to the fire site. At about 5:00 p.m., the fire was extinguished, but it had already burned down more than 20 households, totaling 70 to 80 rooms of various sizes. In addition, a newborn baby of the Fan family was also unable to be rescued and was buried in the fire.

Zhuji Kidnappers Executed in Hangzhou 96

The secret agents of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Department arrested two Zhuji kidnappers, Shou Qingnian and the suspected accomplice Shou Qingan, in Chang'an Town, Haining County. After questioning, it was learned that Shou Qingnian, nicknamed "Xiaoyan" (Small Eyes), had a relationship with Shou Xianzhong, the Chief of Xiyuan Township in the same county. On the night of the 25th day of the eleventh lunar month of the previous year, he learned that Shou Xianzhong was going to see a play in Tang Rendin's new village. The suspect gathered six accomplices, carrying guns, and waited for Shou to come out of the theater near the 材 (Cai) Shuyuan (School). They kidnapped him to Laohudong (Tiger Cave) and Wuzhishan (Five Finger Mountain) in Jiangqiancai and demanded 4,000 yuan, which was split among them. Shou received the largest share of the money and then fled to Chang'an, where he was arrested. He was sentenced to death and was executed by firing squad outside Qingbomen at 9:00 a.m. yesterday (22nd) after his identity was verified. Shou Qingan was acquitted and released.

The four gentlemen in Fujian have heard and witnessed the details of this coup in detail and will report to the Central Government in Beijing immediately.

Long Yongxuan Was Forced to Come to Shanghai: The Dagong News Agency reported that since the outbreak of the coup in Fujian Province, the Fuzhou Unified Tax Administration Office under the jurisdiction of the Central Government was confiscated by the so-called People's Government on the 18th, and the affiliated unified tax branch offices were also forcibly taken over. Long Yongxuan, the original director of the office, in order to report the truth to the Central Government, immediately set off for Shanghai, because all unified tax affairs have been taken over by Mai Ming. The Long family and the tax authorities received this telegram yesterday and are expected to arrive in Shanghai in the coming days.

Results of the Bengbu-Xuzhou National Exhibition: Director-General Xu Qiaoqi Expresses Satisfaction 109

The Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of Domestic Goods, in order to promote domestic goods to the countryside, led the Shanghai Domestic Goods Traveling Group to hold domestic goods exhibitions in Bengbu and Xuzhou, giving farmers the concept of recognizing domestic goods and providing manufacturers with opportunities to promote their products. The National Goods Movement was expanded and publicized with concentrated efforts. Now that it has expired and closed, the representatives of the factories, 187 people, led by Ren Suizhi, Zhao Jinsheng, Lu Yichu, etc., took the Pinghu United Train and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning to return to their respective factories for rest. Yesterday, according to Mr. Xu Qiaoqi, the director-general of the association, this association used the remaining work to try to find a way out for the products of various factories, led them to Bengbu and Xuzhou, held a national exhibition for one week each, publicized domestic goods, and awakened the motive for the people to use domestic goods and develop the national ability to save the country. Surprisingly, the two or three merchants in Bengbu were more interested in their rights than in patriotism, and did not understand the great significance of promoting domestic goods. They misunderstood the truth of dumping and were deeply obsessed with superficial interests. They used the opportunity to advocate opposition. Fortunately, Wang Jun, the commander of the Third Army stationed in Bengbu, He Guoliang, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and Zhou Dezhi, the curator of the People's Education Hall, upheld justice and were responsible for protecting and eliminating misunderstandings. The opening ceremony was held as scheduled. All the shops in the city warmly welcomed, purchased goods in batches, and signed contracts for promotion. Farmers came to the meeting to visit, which was especially enthusiastic. The total sales volume was 74,326.26 yuan, and the products of Sanyou Industrial Society, Wuhe Weaving Factory, Limin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, and Meiya Silk Weaving Factory had the largest sales volume. The Xuzhou National Exhibition proceeded smoothly, but it was regrettable that it was adjacent to a fire and there was a money squeeze. Fortunately, preventive measures were taken to avoid losses. Yu Nianci, the county magistrate, Wang Jun, the commander of the Third Army, Long Ciyun, the director of the Political Training Department, Wang Shicai, the director of the Public Security Bureau, Lan Bohua, the chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, Rui Zhenxiang, the member of the County Party Department, and Zhao Guangtao, the director of the Provincial People's Education Hall, provided meticulous protection and assisted in the process, which gave them a lot of convenience. The venue was crowded with visitors every day. The total sales volume was 69,781.47 yuan, especially the products of Hongxin Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Dalong Woolen Factory, Zhanghua Woolen Factory, China Chemical Industry Society, Tianchu MSG Factory, etc., which were very popular among farmers and sold out. Under the situation of social unrest and rural economic bankruptcy, this achievement is deeply gratifying. The work was tense and the spirit was slightly painful, but the service of domestic goods was not spared. After the association's extensive publicity, the merchants in Bengbu and Xuzhou have expressed their sincere cooperation in promoting domestic goods and forming a permanent business place, which is especially gratifying. The representatives of the participating factories will be convened in a few days to report on the progress of the association's affairs and design the organization of the two domestic goods markets.

Economic Commission: Preparing to Form a Grain Control Committee; Committee Member Candidates to be Recruited Equally from Finance and Grain Industries; Hu Mengjia Internally Designated as Chairman 110

Since the implementation of cotton control by Mr. Song Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Commission, it has progressed smoothly. Control committees for other industries such as grain, silk, minerals, and coal also need to be actively pursued for their establishment in due course. A few days ago, Mr. Song specifically convened leaders of the grain industry association in this city, including Gu Xinyi and Zhu Zixiang, at the Shanghai office of the Economic Commission to discuss matters related to the organization of the Grain Control Committee. Opinions were exchanged and discussions were held. It is reported that the organizational methods will be based on the model of the Cotton Control Committee. As for the candidates for the committee members, they will be recruited equally from the financial sector and the grain industry. Hu Mengjia has already been internally designated as the chairman. Other committee members are being sought, and it is planned to formally establish the committee within this year once suitable candidates are found. It is also reported that after the establishment of the committee, its initial work will follow the example of the Cotton Control Committee, first sending personnel to various provinces and cities to conduct on-site investigations into the annual grain production and sales situation, and then proceeding with the adjustment of surpluses and deficits.

Large Quantities of Japanese Ginseng Shipped to Shanghai; Medicine Shops are Watching and Hesitate to Sell; Plans to Sell in Suzhou, Wuxi, Zhenjiang, Nanjing, etc. 111

According to the Xin Xin News Agency, since the truce agreement in North China, the tense atmosphere between China and Japan has temporarily eased. Our country's boycott of Japanese goods has also gradually subsided. Japanese merchants are taking advantage of the opportunity to import inferior goods in large quantities. It was recently learned from reliable sources that Japanese merchants have recently shipped large quantities of inferior ginseng, intending to peddle them to various ginseng and medicine shops in this city. However, due to the precedent of Shen Feng and other eight rice shops buying and selling Japanese rice, these shops are taking a wait-and-see approach and dare not openly sell the ginseng. Seeing that the situation is not favorable, the Japanese merchants have changed their strategy and are particularly enticing unscrupulous merchants to go to Suzhou, Wuxi, Zhenjiang, Nanjing, and other ports to sell the ginseng. In order to dump the goods, they are lowering the prices to attract customers. It is hoped that the various ginseng and medicine shops will pay attention and not be deceived.

Silk Weaving and Silk Brocade Industries Appeal for Prompt Refund of Artificial Silk Re-Export Tax to Rescue Sales of Nanyang Silk and Recover International Trade 113

The Electrical Silk Weaving Factory Industry Association and the Silk Brocade Industry Association of this city, noting the severe decline in overseas silk sales, went to Beijing in June of this year to petition for the refund of the artificial silk tax. The government adopted their request and agreed to provide relief. Recently, sales in the Nanyang region have been hampered because Japanese goods are being sold at lower prices in that area, causing Chinese silk to be unable to compete in sales. Trade has temporarily stalled, and the situation is serious. Therefore, yesterday, the two associations reported the situation to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, requesting a prompt refund of the artificial silk re-export tax in order to reduce prices, provide urgent relief, and rescue international trade. The original petition is recorded below:

Petition for the Nanyang silk sales to be relieved, as the silk weaving industry is on the verge of bankruptcy, and requesting a prompt refund of the artificial silk re-export tax to aid in the rescue of foreign trade. It is true that the associations have previously reported that the silk brocade business is in a precarious situation, and representatives were sent on June 6 of this year to present everything in person and request the refund of the artificial silk re-export tax to aid in the rescue of overseas silk sales. Subsequently, the Ministry issued Order No. [missing number], which stated [original text omitted] besides exempting the full text from record, the end stated that if the merchants in the industry could specially form a factory that is convenient for customs management, negotiate with customs to establish a bonded manufacturing method, the cost of products can actually be reduced, which is also convenient for foreign trade. This order is hereby notified. Upon receiving this order, we investigated and planned to establish bonded warehouses for manufacturing goods to reduce the burden of products. This was originally the government's intention to care for the hardships of merchants. It could have been without endless complaints. Subsequently, after repeated consideration by the associations, it was unanimously believed that the silk weaving industry, having survived this catastrophe, is only barely surviving to this day. How can we plan for further development? Furthermore, the regulations for this bonded warehouse for manufacturing goods have not yet been established. If we wait for negotiations to be completed, it may not be a matter of a day or two. However, the decline of national silk brocade is like a stack of eggs. How can we delay the rescue? Recently, sales of Chinese silk brocade in the Nanyang region have been hampered. The reason is that Japan, seeing that we have repeatedly increased heavy taxes, resulting in high costs, has taken the opportunity to reduce prices and dump goods as much as possible, in order to compete with our country in international industry and commerce, resulting in Chinese silk brocade being unable to compete in sales, and foreign trade has suddenly stopped. Looking back at the domestic market, it is even more eroded by foreign goods, and the bankruptcy of rural areas. The current situation of silk sales is that there is no escape from losses. In this way, the business is already in extreme danger. If we do not urgently seek relief, then the opportunity for bankruptcy is imminent. Thinking of this, how can we not be worried? The government's plan to save the country should prioritize promoting industry. Therefore, when the Shanghai-Wuxi silk factory closed down, it was specially allowed to issue 4 million yuan in relief bonds. Recently, when yarn factories were in a panic, cotton and wheat loans were used to subsidize them. It can be seen that the government cares for the hardships of the people in every possible way. Today, many silk weaving factories in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are closed, and the number of unemployed workers is no less than that of silk and yarn factories. Although we dare not follow the example of asking for the issuance of public bonds, and even less do we seek loans to rescue industry, the associations, being alert to their own interests, appeal for the refund of the artificial silk re-export tax to relieve the urgent crisis. This should not be an excessive request. Otherwise, once silk weaving goes bankrupt and workers lose their jobs, it will be too late to try to rescue them after the situation has deteriorated to the point of collapse. The difference between success and failure will be far apart. Therefore, we are submitting this joint petition to further describe the obstructed sales of Nanyang silk. We beseech you to examine and approve our request, considering that silk weaving is in danger, and approve the refund of the artificial silk re-export tax in order to aid in the rescue of foreign trade and maintain the employment of workers. We cannot express our pressing need to await orders enough.

Electricity Workers Resume Work at the Factory Yesterday; Order is Good and No Incidents Occurred 114

The Shanghai electricity labor dispute has been temporarily resolved after Mr. Fei Xidun and Mr. Du Yuesheng officially mediated with the company and negotiated several times. All workers in the new and old plants resumed work yesterday morning. The order was good and no incidents occurred. The details are recorded below:

Resumption of Work: Since Mr. Fei Xidun and Du Yuesheng officially started mediation, and after Chinese directors Yuan Ludeng, Yu Qiaqing, Xu Xinliu, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, and Ku Yanfang agreed on the preconditions, all workers, in consideration of public safety and stability, and in obedience to the advice of the mediators, decided to resume work yesterday morning. At 7 a.m. yesterday morning, workers from the new and old plants successively entered the plants to resume work. The company was deeply concerned that there might be temporary changes, so it specially asked the police to send detectives to protect the factory entrances. The order of the workers was good, and no incidents occurred. More than 50 workers were not allowed back to work so they did not resume work. The original mediators will be responsible for negotiating with the company to obtain severance pay and bonuses.

Company Notice: The Shanghai Electric Power Company posted the resumption of work measures at the gates of the old factory on Feilun Road and the new factory on Dongting Road the first night. The translation reads: "Notice to the workers of the Shanghai Electric Power Company: Our company now stipulates the following two measures for resumption of work: (1) All workers employed by the company tomorrow (i.e., the 22nd) will continue to be paid the benefits or rights they were entitled to before, without any changes. (2) Any worker who wishes to borrow money from the company can borrow one month's salary. The borrowed money will be deducted from the salary earned each month at 10% until it is paid off. The remaining wages owed to the workers will be paid off. November 21, 1933. Xue Erde, Deputy General Manager and General Manager."

New Edition of the Postal Atlas of China Published 124

The Postal Bureau recently published the third edition of the Postal Atlas of China. It measures 24 inches in length and 15 inches in width, with 3,000 maps inside. All maps have been revised to 1933. The price is 12 yuan per volume. It is sold in all Postal Administrations and first-class bureaus. Other second-class or third-class bureaus can also order it on behalf of customers. The atlas not only indicates all postal bureaus in the country but also includes detailed information on the distances between bureaus, as well as various postal routes using railroads, ships, airplanes, automobiles, and overland transportation. The atlas is specially made for postal use, and only a small number are available for public purchase.

The Cable Construction of the Telephone Bureau Renovation is Completed; The Third Phase of the Expansion of Relay Equipment Plan; Installation of the Cross-River Line to be Completed Within this Week 128

Since the Traffic Department's Shanghai Telephone Bureau officially launched the automatic telephone system in April of this year, urban traffic has been improving day by day. In order to develop group-run businesses and do its best to serve the public, the bureau has been actively building branch bureaus in various districts and expanding lines. Yesterday, engineer Yu Jian told the Dagong News reporter in detail about the various renovations in Zhabei and the increase in relay equipment. The details are recorded below:

Zhabei Cable Project 129

Since the January 28 Incident in Shanghai the year before last, all lines in Zhabei were destroyed by artillery fire. After the end of the military operations, the bureau formulated a three-stage project for restoration and expansion in order to restore traffic. The first stage was to reorganize the Ming line of Tanziwan and install 50 pairs of cables to and from the Central Mint of Xiaoshadu, starting from the Zhabei branch bureau, and 25 pairs of round trip lines from the Central Mint to Fanwangdu. The project has been completed, and the reorganization of the area around Xingjiaqiao is currently underway. The second phase is to replace the telephone poles, and the third phase is to expand the lines near the area of cross-border road construction in the northern district of the Chinese concession.

Increase Relay Equipment 130

There are a total of 30 pairs of telephone lines from the Zhabei Branch to the Nanshi Headquarters. After the municipal government moves to the central urban area in the future, the Zhabei Branch will occupy an important position in transportation. It is now planned to appropriately increase the relay equipment of all branch bureaus and the concession area. Moreover, there are many users near Yuejie Road who are requesting to install telephones, and the original lines are not enough to allocate. The bureau plans to increase the capacity as much as possible in the third phase of the expansion plan. The materials required have been approved by the Ministry of Transportation, and the Material Purchasing Committee has been ordered to procure them.

Cross-River Line to be Installed 131

The two underwater cross-river lines from Fuzhou Road Waitan to Pudong Lannidu and from Gaochangmiao to Pudong Zhoujiadu started to be installed the day before yesterday. The bottom line from Gaochangmiao to Zhoujiadu will continue to be installed the day after tomorrow, and the work will be completed in about a week.

Accidental Firing; Security Guard Injured 132

Li Jinshan, a security guard from Shandong in the Guanghua Oil Depot in the Jiangxinsha area behind Gaoqiao District in Pudong, is 31 years old and has been serving in the security team for two years. He has been competent in his duties. Yesterday afternoon, Zhang Yongshi, a colleague from Tianjin, who is 35 years old, was rubbing a handgun in the security team's headquarters. Unexpectedly, there was a bullet left in the barrel, and it accidentally fired, shooting Li's right leg and breaking his ankle bone. The bullet is still lodged in the tibia. He was later sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment by his companions.

Lu Baolin Sues Lu Songlin and Others for Property Division; The Case was Dismissed Yesterday 133

Lu A-kui, a Ningbo native residing at No. 32 Mingyueli, Qiwupu Road, is now old. When he was in his thirties and forties, because his wife, Zhang, had not given birth to a child, he adopted a son named Songlin to continue the family line. Later, Zhang unexpectedly gave birth to a daughter, named Yuelin, whom she cherished more than anything. After she grew up, they could not bear to marry her off, so they brought in a son-in-law to live at home in order to be near to her parents. Recently, A-kui's wife passed away, and he himself is declining. His wish has been fulfilled, and his daughter is able to support herself, so he passed on the responsibility of managing the household to his children, and distributed his accumulated property equally. From then on, he could live out his remaining years in peace. But suddenly, Lu Baolin, claiming to be the real daughter of Lu A-kui and Lu Zhang, filed a lawsuit against Lu Songlin and Lu Yuelin for property division. According to her statement, her parents had two daughters, Yuelin being the elder and she being the younger. On the 23rd day of the first month of the lunar calendar in 1923, she married Hua Miaofu with her father's consent. She had gold rings, gold bracelets, gold lockets, gold necklaces, pearl flowers, and other ornaments, which were all stored with her mother. After her mother passed away, the defendants, who lived with her mother, took advantage of their proximity and not only seized the right to manage the family property but also appropriated her stored ornaments. She repeatedly asked for their return, but they always evaded. Now they are taking advantage of the fact that her elderly father is weak and cowardly, arbitrarily dividing the father's property and infringing on her due rights, which is a violation of the law. Therefore, she filed a lawsuit, asking the court to confirm that she has the right of inheritance and order the defendants to hand over all the illegally divided property and redistribute it according to law, with her and her sister each receiving two shares and Songlin receiving one share, and to return the concealed ornaments. Lu's brother and sister replied that it was fortunate that their elderly father was still alive and could easily clarify matters, so in addition to retaining lawyer Chen Tingrui to argue that their parents had longed for a daughter for a long time without success, and only then adopted Songlin to continue the family line and gave birth to Yuelin and brought in a son in law, there was no birth of the plaintiff, now the mother has passed away, the father is still alive, and relatives can also prove, the world is absolutely impossible not to recognize the daughter, that is, take a step back, if Baolin is really Yuelin's sister, then in 1929, when Songlin and Yuelin had litigation over the division of property, why not come out and claim rights, or participate in the litigation, now suddenly ask for the division of property, and demand the custody of jewelry, really do not know what is based on, if you impersonate your daughter with this unfounded thing and intend to divide the property, then there are a little more people in the future, to recognize as a biological child of the person, do not know how much more and so on, in addition, his father Lu A-kui at each first special area court opened the trial, are to the case solemnly prove that the plaintiff Lu Baolin is not his biological daughter, The case has now been investigated and concluded, and yesterday Judge Shen Hong ruled that the plaintiff's lawsuit was dismissed, and the litigation costs were borne by the plaintiff.

The Xiangfeng Company Disregards Debt Case and Creates a Crime of Obstructing Official Duty 134

The shareholder of Xiangfeng Miscellaneous Grain Shop, Shang Zuchen, located at No. 2 Ping'an Lane, Yong'an Street, French Concession, was previously sued by Xiangmao Foreign Firm in the First Special District Court for disregarding debt. Unexpectedly, the manager of the shop, Chen Jikang, and the accountant, Zhou Yixuan, firmly refused, and even verbally abused clerk Chen and other public officials, calling them robbers. Clerk Chen, finding them unreasonable, went to the Da Zimingzhong Police Station to report and request the dispatch of several police officers. Only then were Chen and Zhou taken to the Second Special District Court. Chen Jikang testified that the merchants had never argued with public officials and equivocated about the rest.
