Taikoo's Chongqing Ship Suffers Crane Accident, Killing a Chinese Laborer and Injuring Two Others 135

Taikoo Steamship Company's ship Chongqing, yesterday morning at the company's wharf No. 2 in the French Concession, suffered the tragedy of a Jiangnan Shipyard boiler, the breaking of a ship's mast, the death of a worker, and the dropping of the boiler into the water. The details of this incident are described below.

100,000 Sacks of Flour Shipped to Tianjin 136

The Taikoo Company's sea vessel Chongqing, 2,171 tons, was urgently shipping 100,000 sacks of flour from Shanghai to Tianjin. The ship was berthed at the company's wharf No. 2 in the French Concession for loading. At the same time, Jiangnan Dockyard had a boiler weighing 25 tons, which was also to be transported by the Chongqing ship to Tianjin for unloading. At 9 a.m. yesterday, the boiler was being loaded onto the ship at wharf No. 2 when, unexpectedly, the lifting hook's capacity was exceeded, causing the mast to break, resulting in the accident.

Crane Installation Causes Disaster 137

The boiler transported by Jiangnan Factory was huge in weight and size. It was impossible to lift the 25-ton object onto the ship by manpower alone. At 9 a.m., the workers on the barge used a winch to lower the lifting crane and secured the boiler with steel wire ropes. They immediately started lifting it onto the ship. Unexpectedly, just as the crane was lifting the boiler onto the forward deck of the Chongqing ship, it suddenly crashed into the forward mast during a turn, causing it to break due to the heavy pressure, and immediately fall down. The boiler on the crane fell into the Huangpu River.

Broken Mast Kills Worker 138

The forward mast of the Chongqing ship was made of iron, more than forty feet high, and extremely strong. At that time, the mast was broken and fell down because of the weight of the boiler on the crane. The momentum was terrible, and some of the workers on the deck were unable to escape. A temporary dock worker named Xiao Naijin was killed on the spot, and two other workers were injured, one with a crushed leg and the other with a foot injury. The boiler fell into the Huangpu River, and the mast also fell on the boat.

Damaged Freight Barge 139

When the mast fell, a civil boat named Zhao, which was carrying flour and docked outside, also suffered damage to the deck planks from the falling mast. More than forty bags of flour inside the boat were damaged. A boatman on board was also injured by the mast but fortunately his injuries were minor and not life-threatening. The two seriously injured and leg-fractured workers were sent to Renji Hospital by the dock patrol for treatment. The body of the worker who was killed was taken by the Life Saving Bureau to the morgue for inspection before being collected for burial.

Jesson Salvages Furnace and Mast 140

After this tragedy occurred, the Taikoo Company urgently reported to Jesson Old Dockyard, and dispatched a large crane to Taikoo Wharf No. 2, trying to lift the broken mast. They then used a winch to lift the large boiler out of the water. However, the Chongqing ship could not stay in Shanghai for long because it was in a hurry to go to Tianjin. The company agreed with Jesson to install a temporary mast base first, so that it could go abroad in time. The Chongqing ship has been scheduled to enter the yard this morning to rush the installation of the mast.

Return to Shanghai for Major Repairs 141

The Chongqing ship has been delayed for a day due to this incident, and will not be able to leave Shanghai for Tianjin until tomorrow morning. After the urgently needed 100,000 bags of flour arrive in Tianjin, it will sail back to Shanghai and enter the dock for major repairs, replacing the broken mast and steel cables. At present, it is only temporarily repaired.

Surveyor's Inspection 142

After this incident, due to insurance and other issues regarding the various damages, the Taikoo Company, as usual, reported to the surveyors after the accident to investigate the situation at Wharf No. 2, inquire about the cause of the accident, and take photos for future reference. All the procedures were completed by the afternoon. As for the handling of the dead and injured workers, nothing has been heard yet.

According to yesterday's Japanese-language "Mainichi Shimbun", Akiyama Yonekura, a criminal who used secret wireless telegraphs to disrupt the financial markets in Tianjin, Shanghai, and Dalian in an attempt to make huge profits, (native of Tokyo City, Nakasendo Machi) currently residing at 4-207 Naniwa Machi, Dalian, owner of Nakamura Gakki Store, Nakano Kyuhachi (native of Ishikawa Prefecture, Japan, residing in Akiyama's home, wireless technician), Hiraoka Takao (native of Kyoto, Japan) currently residing in the Qingdao Central Hotel, etc., colluded with Chinese Tianjin Yufeng Bank clerk Ji Hongjun, Zhaoyuan Company manager Wang Chengzhang, clerk Li Encheng, etc., and have been arrested by the Dalian Maritime Police Department's judicial department. The Haikinbo Grand Circus is About to Leave Shanghai, Scheduled to Go to India on the 3rd of Next Month 145

The German Haikinbo Grand Circus, the world's most famous circus, has been performing in Shanghai for a month and a half, and is always fully booked. Each show has twenty programs, which are very exciting and moving. The equestrian stunts, somersaults on wooden poles, lion and tiger mixed performances, aerial acrobatics, etc., are now scheduled to leave Shanghai for India at the beginning of next month. There are only seven or eight days left in China, and there is no definite date for when they will come to China again. Those who have not seen it, please do not miss this last opportunity.

[P>Preferential Viewing for Students<P]

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued an order to the city's primary and secondary schools yesterday, stating that the school had previously reported that students would visit the horse farm or zoo. The bureau had sent personnel to contact the Haikinbo Circus, and decided that on the 25th of this month (Saturday), a special circus performance will be held for the city's primary and secondary school students from 2 pm to 4 pm. The zoo can be visited at any time, with a limit of 400 people each time. Each school can directly contact the circus. Tickets for the circus should be collected at the Accounting Office of the Bureau before 4:30 pm on the 24th of this month with the previously issued receipt. All those who have registered and paid but do not go to visit will not have their money refunded. Each school should provide its own transportation and be properly taken care of by teachers. Students from each school should wear uniforms or Boy Scout uniforms in principle, and should abide by order and pay attention to hygiene. This visit to the circus or zoo has educational significance, and teachers from each school should make good use of the opportunity to arouse children's interest in studying natural sciences. This order is hereby urgently issued for compliance.

Fiji to Ban Import of Chinese Ham, Plans to Formulate Meat Import Regulations, Chinese Ham Merchants to Suffer Greatly 157

When Wen Jiang and others of the Philippine Industrial Inspection Group came to Shanghai this spring, the local International Trade Bureau and Commodity Inspection Bureau successively received them and led them to visit various industrial factories, hoping that trade between China and Fiji could be increased after the group returned home. Unexpectedly, after the group returned home, they considered that major commodities exported from our country to Fiji, such as ham, were manufactured in an unsanitary manner, and suggested that the government ban the import of our country's ham. After repeated negotiations by our consul-general in Manila, Yun Guanglin, no effect was seen, and it was learned that the local health bureau had drafted meat import regulations and submitted them to the Fiji governor for approval. If these regulations are implemented, our country's ham industry to Fiji will inevitably be greatly affected. The following is the transcript of the report of the Consul-General to Manila, Li Guanglin, on this matter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, to illustrate the exclusion of Chinese goods. I have investigated that meat products made in our country are sold to Fiji Island, amounting to 1.1 million pesos (Dutch currency) annually, accounting for more than one-tenth of the imported goods. American merchants and the Fiji government have long regarded this as a major loophole and have always wanted to restrict it. Such as the council repeatedly proposing tax increase bills and the health bureau pointing out poor manufacturing methods, are all caused by this. However, because this kind of food is favored by Chinese and Fiji people and the price is cheaper than American goods and local exports, it has been able to maintain sales. The Fiji government advocates restricting the import of Chinese ham and meat products, because the director of the health bureau, Fuhart, former director of the livestock bureau, Yang Bai, and director of the livestock bureau, Pu Kemi, Pu Kemi also has a large investment in the local meat industry, and he holds it especially firmly. In April of this year, Fuhart, Yang Bailuti, went to Shanghai and other places to inspect the equipment of our country's ham and meat production. After returning to Fiji, they cited that the manufacturing method was unsanitary and feared hindering people's health, and asked the Fiji governor to order a ban on imports from 1934. Those shipped this year are limited to no more than 50,000 pieces from the Shanghai Chinese Ham Company, and no more than 500 pieces from L. Adams Ce. After the official met with the Fiji Governor's Health Advisor Denham and the members of the House of Representatives Wen Jiang and Lunna, who went to China in March of this year to inspect business, explained that this ham and meat had been eaten by Fiji people for a long time and had no hindrance to health. Stopping the import and reducing tariffs would be harmful. The advisor and others expressed sympathy. Later, the Governor also considered that it would hinder the freedom of Sino-Fiji trade and did not agree. In fact, the government relies on this meat to collect import duties, as well as direct and indirect business taxes, amounting to 400,000 pesos per year. Once the import is banned, it will be replaced by tax-free American goods. At a time when the Fiji government is facing financial difficulties, it is especially unwilling to give it up. Now the director of the health bureau, Fuhart, follows the authorities' intentions and plans to formulate a meat import regulation and submit it to the Fiji governor for approval. This example is based on the German method of dealing with the United States in those years, (according to the years 1896, Germany once banned American ham from entering the country, and later the United States allowed it to be manufactured according to its regulations before it was restored,) In Fiji, apart from those from the United States and Australia, Chinese goods are the most imported ham and meat, and it is obvious that it is set up for our country. The drafting of this regulation is intended by the authorities, and it seems to be imperative. This regulation is very detailed on the procedures for manufacturing ham and meat, and is in line with hygiene principles. With the current equipment of our country's companies, it seems not difficult to improve, but its use as a standard for domestic products is allowed as a way for the government to pay attention to hygiene, as the regulations that should be followed when manufacturing imported goods, not without Yue Zu official. I also met with consultant Denham and told him that our country is willing to improve the manufacturing method of ham and meat in order to increase foreign sales. This example is quite valuable and will be presented for reference. If there are any improvements better than our country, we will be happy to adopt them. However, whether our country accepts it or not, sufficient time should be given in advance for detailed study. The consultant agreed with this point. The equipment of the Fiji factory is far inferior to our country, and the output is not much and the quality is also inferior, but it is now engaged in improvement and progress is very rapid. At present, the Fiji government has formulated a good manufacturing method, and it seems that it should be adopted, otherwise, even if it is not prohibited from being imported because it does not comply with the manufacturing, Fiji goods may also encroach on sales. This matter concerns an important business case, and it is reasonable to copy four copies of the draft regulations and present them to you for your review, and ask to forward them to the Ministry of Industry, issue them to the International Trade Bureau, and conduct a commodity inspection to avoid them. Please indicate how to handle it. Respectfully presented to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Consul-General to Manila, Kuang Guanglin.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Urges Paper Industry to Purchase Yellow Hollyhock for Papermaking to Rescue Collapsing Rural Economy 158

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to the Paper Industry Guild, stating: "Dear Sirs, We received a letter on the 21st of this month from the Nanhui County Government, forwarded from Zhang Bangjie, District Chief of the Sixth District of your county, who presented a report from Hu Pinchun, Township Head of Zhu Dian Township, stating: 'Farmers in various townships of this district, recognizing the consecutive years of poor harvests and low prices of cotton, rice, and wheat, are now switching to planting yellow hollyhock, as it is more profitable. They eagerly sought seeds priced at three yuan per catty and followed suit in planting this spring. Furthermore, Mr. Tianxu Wo Sheng from Shanghai wrote a leaflet, distributed by Ding Zhen Dong from Chuansha, promoting planting to remedy the agricultural situation. The planting methods, uses, and sales channels were explained in detail, taking its roots as a raw material for papermaking. Factories in Shanghai have a substantial annual demand. Upon harvest, the farmers in this district approached various paper mills for sales, but were met with claims of market saturation and refusal to purchase. Whether still in the fields or already harvested and piled up, the yellow hollyhock is vulnerable to frost and sun, leading to rot and becoming useless. The farmers are in panic, and the Township Head, witnessing this situation, believes that the rural economy is on the verge of collapse. If no measures are taken to remedy this, the farmers will suffer even more, which concerns the national economy and the people's livelihood. Therefore, we are writing to the County Government, requesting them to consult with paper mills and related organizations in Shanghai to urgently purchase the yellow hollyhock as much as possible to benefit the farmers' livelihoods, etc.' Based on this, in addition to the order, we are correspondingly requesting your esteemed association to investigate and instruct the paper mills to purchase as much as possible to rescue the collapsing rural economy. It is said that yellow hollyhock is a raw material for papermaking adhesive, and Shanghai factories have a substantial annual demand. There have been reports of prominent figures in the papermaking industry promoting planting. The farmers of Nanhui have actively responded. If they are refused purchase, it would be a waste of resources and further hasten rural bankruptcy. We are accordingly requesting your esteemed association to earnestly persuade member paper mills to raise funds and purchase as much as possible to maintain the livelihoods of the farmers and prevent them from abandoning their profession. This is also to prevent a shortage of raw materials next year, which would indirectly benefit the operations of the factories. We urge you to sincerely persuade them and report the handling situation for further communication. This is our earnest request."

Page 11

Operating Methods of China Economic Credit Cooperative Society Differ from Ordinary Commercial and Financial Industries - Members Can Manage Funds and Review Investments - Society Funds Will Be Increased to 500,000 Yuan in Installments 159

The China Economic Credit Cooperative Society at 455 Hankou Road in this city has been well-received by the public since its opening. However, many outside parties do not understand its operating methods. A gentleman made a special inquiry and learned the general outline: (1) Characteristics of Economic Cooperation: Economic cooperation has two characteristics: First, using the mutual assistance of the public to exchange the greatest benefits at the least cost. Second, the principle is to trust oneself and manage and use funds independently. Ordinary financial industries do not use capital to pay interest or claims. For example, the interest paid by banks to depositors is only the income from the use of their deposits. Other examples include the death benefits paid by insurance companies, which are only jointly borne by the insured. In fact, they are all examples of cooperation and mutual assistance by making good use of deposits and insurance. In addition to paying interest and claims, ordinary financial industries also have huge profits. Cooperative societies allow members to directly enjoy this type of profit. In other words, members share the greatest benefits because of mutual assistance. The most important part of financial institutions is the management of funds and investment review. Depositors cannot intervene in this process. Recognizing this, the Society has established a Fund Management Committee and an Investment Review Committee to execute supervision and review investment funds. In addition to the Chairman and General Manager of the Society serving as natural committee members, the majority of the members of these two committees are selected from among the members of the Society. Members account for an absolute majority and have the power to manage and review without bearing the responsibility for business losses. This is unmatched by any financial institution. (2) The Use and Increase of the Society's Funds: The characteristics of economic cooperation are such that the Society's funds are used for expenses and guarantees. The use of the Society's funds is also based on this, rather than seeking huge profits like commercial and financial industries, or consolidating the faith of depositors. Since the use of the Society's funds is for (1) expenses and (2) guarantees, a huge amount of capital is not required in the first phase. It is only necessary for the Society's funds to cover expenses and for the total amount of the Society's funds to be sufficient for guarantees. From now on, the Society's expenses will be maintained with the Society's fund income. The estimated number of Society members in the first phase is 5,000 shares, so the 100,000 yuan liability of the first phase of the Society's funds is sufficient for guarantee. From then on, for every 1,000 shares increased, the liability increases by 5,000 yuan until it reaches 500,000 yuan. (3) The Society's Funds and the Role of Capital in Commercial and Financial Industries Are Different: The Society is different from ordinary businesses. Ordinary businesses use capital to seek huge profits, and these profits come from customers. The Society's core members do not seek this kind of benefit. The Society is also different from the financial industry. The financial industry must have a large amount of capital to consolidate the faith of depositors. Since the Society is managed independently by members, this is not necessary. Comparing safety, the Society's members are better than bank depositors. Any general bank's capital is not proportional to the deposits it absorbs. A bank with 5 million yuan of capital often has over 50 million yuan in deposits. The guarantee obtained by depositors is only one-tenth in terms of capital ratio. It is ultimately not as safe as the Society's members being able to manage it themselves. (4) The Guarantee Responsibility of the Society's Core Members: In addition to contributing capital, the Society's core members must also bear a guarantee responsibility. If the person dies or the business fails midway, they cannot be held responsible. Recognizing this, the Society will pay the savings life fund for those who should have received six percent dividends. Even if the person dies or becomes unemployed midway, there is no need to worry. (5) The Handling of Members' Savings and the Benefits Enjoyed: One might ask where the generous benefits enjoyed by the Society's members come from and how the savings turned over by the Society's members are handled. Originally, the Society took one-tenth of the members' savings to use for members' dormitories, reception rooms, entertainment rooms, reading rooms, employment agencies, and various consultant guidance committees. The remaining nine-tenths were turned over to the Fund Management Committee every afternoon for management, and the Investment Review Committee carefully invested it. The income was used to guarantee the payment of members' bonuses, claims, and principal and interest. If there are not enough, the Society's funds will be allocated. If it is still not enough to pay, it is guaranteed by the guarantee amount. (6) The Relationship Between the Society and Members Can Be Determined Independently: The relationship between the Society's members and the Society can be chosen by the members. In order to enable members to join shares for free in the future, all those who join the Society as members can allocate the dividends they should receive to pay for share subscriptions (those who do not wish to do so may listen). Therefore, anyone who joins the Society not only enjoys life insurance, savings, bonuses, loans, entertainment, and mutual assistance benefits, but also becomes a member of the Society after a considerable number of years, jointly bearing the responsibility for management.

Wet Nurse, Resenting Termination of Employment, Feeds Child Needles; Case Continues Trial; Police Prosecute for Attempted Murder; Defense Lawyer Presents Three Points of Suspicion 169

Wu Xiaoke, a native of Fujian, courtesy name Ruichai, residing at No. 5 Xuehuali Road in the French Concession, currently a civil judge in the Second Special District Court, and his wife had a daughter, named Xiaomeimei, in May of this year in the lunar calendar. Recently, due to insufficient breast milk, they hired Chen Tang, a young woman from Yangzhou (26 years old this year), through the Xinji Li Matchmaker Agency at the intersection of Ximen Malang Road as a wet nurse on the 10th of last month. After a successful trial, a monthly salary of nine yuan was agreed upon and two months' salary was prepaid. However, not long after starting work, she suddenly requested leave to go out and play, but the owner refused because the child needed to be breastfed every day. She became unhappy and suddenly showed her explosive temper, often beating the child. Until the 10th of this month, Wu's wife saw Tang beating the child, so she was dismissed immediately and ordered to return the prepaid salary for one month. The matchmaker was told to take her away and another wet nurse was hired. Unexpectedly, Tang resented this and secretly fed the child three lead-wire iron needles, in an attempt to vent her anger. After swallowing the needles, the child suddenly fell ill and cried non-stop. The parents did not understand, so they sent the child to the hospital for treatment. After examination by the doctor, the cause of the illness was also unclear, so they took the child back and extended the treatment to a pediatrician, Xu Xiaopu. At noon on the 12th, when the child urinated, Wu's wife and another wet nurse discovered one bent iron needle each at the child's anus. Only then did they realize that Tang had plotted and used this vicious method. They reported it to the French police. Detective Peng Shitian went to investigate and personally took out a lead-wire needle from the child's anus and arrested Tang. During interrogation, she admitted without hesitation that she had fed the child the needles while breastfeeding. The next day, when she was escorted to the Second Special District Court for a hearing, she cunningly denied it again. She was ordered to be detained pending further investigation. The details have been recorded in previous newspapers. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the continued hearing in Criminal Court No. 1. First, the police lawyer Fei Xizhen stated the police investigation process and prosecuted her for attempted murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Law. The plaintiff did not arrive. When questioned, the defendant Chen Tang continued to cunningly deny it. Then, Yu Zhongluo, the lawyer appointed by the court to defend the defendant, stood up and expressed his opinion, stating that there were three points of suspicion in this case: (1) The child defecates every day. Why was it only after two days that the needles were swallowed and discovered in the stool? (2) According to the report, the defendant put the needle on the nipple and fed it to the child. According to the detective's report, the defendant first put the needle in the child's mouth and then fed it during breastfeeding. (3) Since the defendant has been dismissed and is not allowed to take care of the child, she has already left the child. How could she have the opportunity to poison her again? According to these three points of suspicion, the court should conduct a detailed investigation, etc. After verifying the words, the court ordered that the hearing be adjourned to the 27th. The defendant was still detained.

Four Banks Joint Treasury Issues Reserve Report, No. 203 182

The Four Banks Joint Treasury, jointly established by the Y盐业, Jincheng 金城, Zhongnan 中南, and Dalu 大陆 Banks, is dedicated to issuing banknotes for the Zhongnan Bank. A public announcement is made weekly, audited by auditors and accountants from the four banks. Breakdown: Cash reserves: 21,411,837 yuan. Security reserves: 5,920,100 yuan.

City News 184

Establishment of the Saint Anna Dance Academy: Several prominent figures in Shanghai's social circles have joined forces with renowned American musicians White Smith and Sang Meng, along with numerous dance experts, to establish the "Saint Anna Dance Academy." Wang Xinhe and Yu Kefei, owners of the Saint Anna Dance Hall, have been appointed to manage the academy. The academy's location has been chosen as the lower level of the Saint Anna Dance Hall on Jing'an Temple Road near Xieqiao Road. It is reported that the academy's establishment is entirely aimed at elevating the status of social dancing. Therefore, renowned experts have been hired to participate in the academy's educational activities. After the academy opens, membership will be extremely selective. The grand opening ceremony is scheduled for December 1st, at which time White Smith and prominent figures from Shanghai will be invited to attend the opening ceremony, which will be enlivened by a tea dance.

The Security Door Viewer that Has Created a Sensation Throughout Shanghai: The domestic Security Door Viewer issued by the Security Door Viewer Company at 551 Nanjing Road, Continental Emporium, was invented by industrialists Sang Yutang and Yu Jiesheng. The mirror is placed on the door, allowing a clear view of everything outside the door from the inside. Even if someone is hidden in the corner, they cannot escape detection. However, those outside cannot see anything inside. The viewer prevents burglars, swindlers, and robberies, and avoids unnecessary social engagements. Since its introduction just a week ago, it has created a sensation throughout Shanghai. Not only have mansions and residences, such as those of Huang Jinrong, Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Fang Jiaobo, Chen Zhaqing, Yang Xiaotian, Lu Wenshao, Lu Ying, Jiang Yiping, Yan Duhe, Xi Yushu, Zheng Chengqing, and Gu Zhuxuan, already installed them, but also banks such as the Silk Industry Bank and the Women's Bank have successively installed them. Furthermore, law offices, doctors' surgeries, shop accounting offices, factory offices, and schools are all actively contacting the company to install them as soon as possible. Shops in other cities are eagerly seeking to become exclusive distributors. Major department stores such as the China National Products Company, Sincere, Wing On, and Foo An are also experiencing significant sales. This is truly good news for the domestic goods industry, which has been in a slump for years.

Recent News from the China National Products Agency: The China National Products Agency has been operating for over a month, and its recent work has become even more intensive. To facilitate joint production and sales and to respond to requests for guidance from various agencies and schools, the agency has dispatched specialists to actively promote and handle domestic goods. Shanghai has been divided into South Shanghai, North Shanghai, West Shanghai, East Shanghai, and Central Shanghai, with the specialists departing separately. Contacts have already been made, and agencies and schools in South Shanghai and Central Shanghai have been very supportive. All inquiries about domestic goods are being answered in detail to the best of their knowledge.

Xia Ziyi's Lotus Silk Seal Inkpad: Xia Ziyi of Jiangdu has been fond of epigraphy since childhood and has collected many rubbings from stone inscriptions. He especially enjoys making seal inkpads and has been meticulously studying this art for over twenty years, finally achieving success. His handmade inkpads are all as red as cinnabar, with a pearly luster that dazzles the eyes. They are truly unprecedented masterpieces. The best of these are made with lotus silk, and connoisseurs who obtain them cherish them as treasures, respectfully calling them the "Inkpad Emperor." The next best is made with wild mugwort down, divided into eight grades: Divine, Exquisite, High, Fine, Super, Excellent, Superior, and Good. Recently, in response to requests from enthusiasts, he has agreed to sell them in Shanghai. He currently resides at the Xiyin Study, No. 19 Furun Alley, at the intersection of Beijing Road and Guizhou Road. His Superior and Good grades are priced very affordably, making them suitable for use in commercial seals. In addition to making inkpads, appraising inscriptions, and tasting tea, Xia Ziyi is skilled in treating external diseases and has secretly concocted effective medicines. If friends are sick and seek treatment, he can always cure them quickly. However, he is unwilling to practice medicine publicly, so patients who wish to seek Xia Ziyi's diagnosis must have a close friend introduce them.

Grand Sale at the Shunfeng Hosiery Factory: The Shunfeng Hosiery Factory in the Qipan Street section of Henan Road is a long-established store in Shanghai, renowned in the city for its genuine goods at fair prices. Recently, the factory has launched a grand, sacrificial 21-day sale to thank its long-time customers, selling its own products regardless of cost. Each customer who spends over three yuan will receive a bottle of Queen's Cream as a gift. Yesterday, the first day of the sale, customers were extremely crowded. Those who purchased goods were delighted by the low prices. It is said that the total sales for the day reached four to five thousand yuan.

The "Huizhou Daily" Expands Its Pages: The "Huizhou Daily" is published in Tunxi, and its circulation has been extremely popular since its inception. Last week, the newspaper's editor, Mr. Bi Zhuojun, visited Shanghai on business, discussing the recent situation in Huizhou in detail. According to Mr. Bi, the newspaper's news and advertising sections are extremely crowded, but the limited space has prevented it from printing everything. To expand its business, it will expand its pages starting on New Year's Day in 1934, publishing one or one and a half large sheets daily. A full-page printing press has already been purchased and shipped to Tunxi. The newspaper has also contacted major advertising companies in Shanghai to receive advertisements from major businesses in Shanghai. A distribution office has been set up on Wangping Street to avoid the inconvenience of ordering newspapers by mail for the Shanghai community.

Weather Report 188

The Xujiahui Observatory issued the following weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: The Shandong coast is clear and calm, with variable winds. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy with fog, with winds from the southwest to northwest. Coastal areas south of Ma'an Island are cloudy, with gentle northeasterly to easterly winds. There is a cyclone in the Yellow Sea, caused by a low-pressure system moving northeast. The hurricane is east of Mindanao, continuing to move west. Its center was within 120 miles of the intersection of 11 degrees North latitude and 133 degrees East longitude at approximately 6:00 AM this morning. The wind force is unknown. Also, in the 24 hours preceding 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in Shanghai reached a high of 73.4 degrees and a low of 51.8 degrees. On the same day last year, the high was 69.3 degrees and the low was 42.4 degrees.

The Jiangsu Provincial Schools Will First Receive Half a Month's Funding; Payment Notices Will Be Issued Soon 190

Payment notices for the September funding for Jiangsu provincial middle schools and normal schools (October for rural normal schools and elementary schools, the second half of September and the first half of October for social education institutions and vocational schools) have been signed by the auditors and sent to the Department of Education for stamping. However, because the treasury had just cleared the August funding for provincial schools and the September funding for rural normal schools and elementary schools, only one to two million yuan in cash remained. It was not convenient to issue bounced checks (if the payment notices were issued first, but the treasury lacked sufficient funds, the bank would not be able to cash them, making them no different from bounced checks), so they were withheld. It is reported that the current treasury balance is over 80,000 yuan. In addition, the educational funds that various counties are submitting one after another are expected to be deposited by the 25th of this month (approximately on the 23rd or 24th). The Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office will first issue payment notices for half a month's funding, and schools and social education institutions can receive half a month's cash after receiving the notices.

The Shanghai University Federation Will Hold a University Student Speech Competition; Preliminary Rounds on December 2nd, Finals on December 9th 193

The university student Mandarin speech competition organized by the Shanghai University Federation has been scheduled for preliminary rounds on December 2nd and finals on December 9th. The registration deadline is the 25th of this month. The latest preparations are detailed below.

Participating Schools: The following schools will participate in this Mandarin speech competition: Guanghua University, Jiaotong University, Daxia University, Jinan University, Fudan University, National Business College, Shanghai University, and Chi Chih College, totaling over ten schools.

Judging Criteria: The judging criteria are divided into four categories: structure, content, delivery, and demeanor. Structure accounts for 30%, content accounts for 30%, delivery accounts for 20%, and demeanor accounts for 20%. Three judges will be invited to each preliminary round, and three different judges will be invited to the finals. The executive committee is currently sending out invitations. The speech results will be calculated by converting the scores given by each judge into rankings and then adding the rankings. The speaker with the lowest total ranking will be the first place winner. If the total rankings are equal, the speaker with the highest total score will be ranked higher.

Solicitation of Prizes: To encourage students from various schools to participate in the speech competition, the executive committee has sent letters to various agencies, schools, and organizations to solicit prizes. The number of prizes awarded will depend on the number of groups in the preliminary rounds. If the preliminary rounds are divided into one or two groups, prizes will be awarded to the top three finishers in the finals. If the preliminary rounds are divided into three groups, prizes will be awarded to the top five finishers in the finals.

Special Article China: An Overview of Modern Educational Thought (5) - Narrated by Shu Xincheng, Notes by Sun Yucai 219

(3) The Period of the New Culture Movement (1919-1923/24): In 1919, due to diplomatic issues, China experienced the May Fourth Movement. The New Culture Movement was conceived in response to this. Because of the advocacy of the New Culture Movement, old morality, old thoughts, and old culture were vehemently criticized. Even Confucius was among those to be overthrown. They believed that China's decline was not merely a matter of political corruption, but resulted from the failure of social thought and social systems. The influence of the New Culture Movement at that time was truly beyond description. The articles written by Chen Duxiu and others in the "New Youth" magazine strongly advocated that China could only be saved through democracy, science, freedom, and liberation. For the sake of clarity, I will categorize the relevant educational thoughts of this period into five aspects for separate explanation.

Vocational Education Thought: Vocational education thought originated from two sources: first, the needs of domestic society; and second, the stimulation of European and American vocational education thought. The term "vocational education" was first coined by Lu Feikui, and the most vigorous promoter afterwards was the Chinese Vocational Education Society. There are varying interpretations and definitions of vocational education. Huang Yanpei said, "Any education method that enables everyone to obtain livelihood and enjoyment, and at the same time fulfill their obligations to the community, is called vocational education." Zou Enrun said, "Vocational education prepares one to master a skill, engage in productive endeavors beneficial to society, and seek a proper life. Its greatest goal is to cultivate one's intellect, will, and emotions, and to become a completely useful person." Speaking of the practical impact of vocational education thought, it was indeed very significant, unmatched by other ideologies. First, it occupied a formal and important position in the new school system. Second, it achieved great success in implementation. Since Huang Yanpei and others founded the Chinese Vocational Education Society in 1917 as an organization for researching and promoting vocational education, they established the Chinese Vocational School to conduct practical experiments. Subsequently, it developed rapidly and vigorously. However, simply advocating vocational education cannot solve the employment problems of the intellectual class. It is necessary to pay attention to political issues and social undertakings, and seek comprehensive and unified progress. Because China's politics are not on track and social undertakings are very underdeveloped, although vocational education thought is constantly advancing and vocational education institutions are increasing daily, the acute employment problem among intellectuals remains unresolved.

Democratic Education Thought: Democratic education is another name for democracy (Democracy) education, or popular education. It originated in the early years of the Republic of China and flourished after 1919. There are three reasons for its great popularity: first, external influence from world trends; second, the influence of the Literary Revolution, during which new ideas were introduced and old ideas were criticized as much as possible. At that time, the democratic thought after the European war was transmitted to China, and everyone could freely accept it without any restrictions; third, the May Fourth Movement, whose purpose was the transformation of politics, was actually the result of the collision of old and new ideas. John Dewey also came to China at this time with his democratic educational philosophy and lectured, supplemented by the vigorous advocacy of Hu Shi and other pioneers of the Chinese Literary Revolution, so democratic educational thought flourished at that time. Its first influence was the destruction of the central centralization system, the adoption of elective courses, and the free experimentation of teaching methods. The second is that women have the same opportunities as men in education. The third is the development of civilian education. The fourth is the close relationship between politics and education. The fifth is the increase in students' power. The above five things are only the greater influences that democratic educational thought has had on practical education in China. In detail, there are naturally more than these. For example, the youth's literary enthusiasm and love enthusiasm are related to this educational thought. But these alone are enough to show the power of this educational thought. During this period, there were only two broad roads in front of us: the first is the cultivation of a scientific spirit, and the second is the promotion of material civilization. The power to lead these two roads naturally lies in the government's education policy. However, every member of the education community has power. I just don’t know what educators think about the state of affairs.

Independent Education Thought: Humans must seek education for their living needs, and because education is a tool to achieve life goals, everyone needs to use this tool to achieve their expected goals. Therefore, the independent thinking of the education community erupted, believing that it was not necessary to rely on the government, so there was a movement of "educational independence." First, it started with the independence of education funding, and later, due to religious and political party issues, various disputes arose in education. Therefore, it extended from the independence of education funding to complete independence from politics and religion in legislation and administration. In fact, strictly speaking, the four characters of educational independence, formed into a noun, are really not very reasonable, but in the history of modern education, there is actually a kind of educational independence thought, which even lasted for ten years in time and filled the whole country in space. Its changes are four: at first, there was the idea of independent education funding due to the arrears of funding; later, because the independence of education funding could not be achieved unless education was separated from the political tide first, it further advocated the independence of education affairs, and further advocated the independence of education from political parties and religions. This is the system of the development of independent educational thought. Outside this system, there is a part of the independence of teachers' personality and academic aspects in higher education. In general, independent educational thought has little practical impact, because education is a part of national administration. Whether the country adopts party politics or non-party politics, those who hold political power naturally want to express their political propositions or policies, and education will naturally be dominated by their policies or propositions. Independence is really difficult to realize.

Scientific Education Thought: In 1921, Paul Monroe of the United States was hired by the Practical Education Investigation Society to investigate education in China and strongly stated that scientific education in China was failing in various ways. The following year, the Education Improvement Society hired an American, Push, to come to China to guide scientific education, and scientific education became very popular. At that time, the scientific education thought was a reflection of foreign insults, and a reflection of the impracticality of the new education. Although it has lasted for more than 30 years in the history of education in China, it has had little impact on practical education. There are two main factors why scientific education is ineffective in China: the first is national habits, and the second is the poison of science. But the need for China to promote scientific education, I am afraid that except for Tagore and other figures who praise Eastern spiritual civilization, there will be no problem. Although we cannot discuss the specific implementation plan here, we can determine that there are two directions for its progress: first, on the positive side, vigorously advocate the Chinese people to work hard to create material civilization and arouse their demand for scientific research; second, on the negative side, vigorously break the current lottery-like bad habit of officials, so that people have to support themselves and indirectly develop science by working hard in production construction.

Non-Religious Education Thought: After the Republic of China, internal turmoil continued, education funding was in arrears for a long time, and education undertakings were also manipulated by warlords and politicians, allowing them to play tricks at will, so that inherent schools could not be maintained, let alone developed, while church schools took advantage of that time to take the opportunity to promote themselves because they were not affected by domestic politics. At that time, the so-called religious education institutions were almost only Christian church schools, so non-religious education simply took non-Christian church schools as the only object. In fact, it is "non" all religious education. After the May Fourth Movement, the people's thinking was greatly liberated, and they re-evaluated the value of everything in society with a skeptical attitude. Everyone believes that education is a tool to study and enlighten the human spirit, and religion is a shackle that forces faith and blocks human wisdom. Education must be separated from religion in order to show its true spirit of free development, so religion and education cannot be combined. At that time, Mr. Cai Yuanpei's theory of aesthetic education replacing religion won people's confidence, and in practice, organizations such as the Non-Religious Grand Alliance and the Non-Christian Grand Alliance were established to engage in fierce action against it. The idea of non-religious education was so serious, and later, due to the new nationalism in politics and the new rationalism in thought as the background, as well as world trends and the turbulence of domestic political groups, the result was that it had a great impact on education. On January 16 of the fourteenth year, the Ministry of Education promulgated the Measures for Requesting Approval for Establishing Schools with Foreign Donations. Its content, on the one hand, paid attention to the recovery of the education school, and on the other hand, paid attention to the independence of education from religion. On the civil side, they urgently sought to break away from education schools and create new schools by themselves. Why can it have such a big impact on education? That is because religious education does not have a deep-rooted foundation in Chinese national thought. Its development completely depends on the oppression of foreign forces and the chaos of internal affairs. Its nature was originally a rootless duckweed, so when it encountered the storm of national movement and rationalism, coupled with the push of world trends and domestic political groups, it had to disappear.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Words of Contribution

Let the Ladies Promote National Goods 220

— Yang An

丨Who controls the vitality of domestic goods? The power lies with the women.丨

We have tried our best to promote domestic products throughout the year. However, like "dancing while carrying a stone mortar," it's hard work without reward. How much benefit has it brought to the domestic product industry? It's truly minimal. This is not surprising, because every family has a housewife, commonly known as the "head of the household," and the power to adopt domestic products lies in their hands. Most male heads of household just talk, make a fuss, give speeches, and join in, which is like useless effort. If you don't believe it, please go to the entrance of the Chinese National Products Company in Shanghai and watch the people coming and going. Are there more male heads of household or female heads of household? Sometimes these female heads of household also listen to their daughters. As long as their daughters say that domestic products are suitable for them and how useful they are, they will happily buy as much as possible for their beautiful daughters and become loyal believers in domestic products. Therefore, the vitality of domestic goods can be said to be completely in the hands of women. In the future, when the bosses of domestic product factories welcome the god of wealth, they must not welcome the male god of wealth, but the female god of wealth. In particular, they must please the many "Jade Emperors" in other people's homes, and flatter the "Guanyin Bodhisattvas" and their sons and daughters. This is not a joke. We have indeed taken some wrong paths in the past, that is, we have failed to mobilize the ladies to promote domestic products, which is a big mistake. If the ladies and daughters are willing to come out with sincerity and promote domestic products, then it will be easy to achieve twice the results with half the effort. Fortunately, at the end of this year, there is finally some good news: the Women's Christian Temperance Union's domestic product exhibition. Their exhibition has swept away the old stereotypes and is completely centered on the family, creating a model domestic product family. From the living room, dining room, bedroom, to the kitchen and toilet, all are decorated and displayed with domestic products, adopting the principles of beauty, economy, tranquility, hygiene, and simplicity, and arranged according to three kinds of budgets based on the amount of each person's economic income. This kind of display can make people have the value of research, which is really in line with scientific methods. The day before yesterday, I heard Ms. Yu Yingjie, the wife of the director of the association, and Ms. Qian say: "I hope that the domestic product factories that send products to the association for display will display them for the domestic product movement, not just for their own convenience." They also said: "This exhibition is not rigid and dead, but fluid and alive. For example, we must come up with good styles for children's clothing and women's fashion, and everyone will criticize and study them together, so that domestic products can progress." Mrs. Yu also said: "Shanghai's use of domestic products is the most important and most effective. If every woman in Shanghai uses domestic products for food and clothing, the trend will be such that people in the interior will probably use domestic products exclusively. If Shanghai people wear domestic silk and cloth, I guarantee that Suzhou and Hangzhou people will wear domestic silk and cloth within a week. Because the people in the interior can be said to completely imitate the people in Shanghai, and Shanghai people have the power to shift the trend." These words all have meaning. It is said that it will open on December 14 at the Association on Yuanmingyuan Road in Shanghai. This is the most gratifying thing in the domestic product year.

Talks on National Products

Domestic Goods and Children's Education 221

— Ba Ling

This year is the year of domestic products. In principle, the results of promoting domestic products should be much more advanced than in the past. In this way, the name is also appropriate, but the facts are placed in front of us, which really makes us very sad. This year, the results of domestic product sales are not seen to be very clever, but Japanese goods are selling and selling especially well in the market. The year of domestic products has created an opportunity for Japanese goods to sell. Isn’t it strange!

Mr. Yan Esheng and Pan Yangyao both said, "This year is the year of the bank," and some people say, "This year is the year of shelving goods," and some people even say, "This year is the year of Japanese goods," which is really an inspiring statement!

From this, it can be seen that to promote domestic products, we still need to do some thorough work and start from the lower level to be effective. Our adults, because our minds are basically full of the mentality of worshiping foreign goods, so the propagandists are all shouting hoarsely, but the effect is very small!

What is the basic work at the lower level? The author believes that promoting domestic products must start with children and publicize to children, so that in the minds of children, from small to large, there is a mentality that only domestic products are bought, and that buying foreign goods is a great shame. If this concept is formed in the minds of every child, I believe that in less than ten years, our national goods will fall without being beaten, and the domestic goods movement will not need to be promoted and promoted by itself.

However, this basic and great work still needs to be done by us adults. Parents should explain to children every day, and be able to set an example by their own actions. At the same time, teachers must also publicize to students at all times, and also set an example by their own actions. Only in this way can the domestic goods movement be completed, and the national economy will have a day of abundance, and the people's lives will be freed from hardship. Otherwise, our national front is not allowed to be optimistic.

Therefore, the promotion of domestic products should go hand in hand with children's education. Readers, after reading my views, I don’t know what you think?

Young People, Stop Being Salesmen for Foreign Goods 222

— Xuan Wan

Is it true that in these few years, the Chinese market is entirely under the occupation of foreign economic forces? Have our excellent young people not tasted enough of this taste of aggression, and are they not aware of the downturn in domestic industry and commerce and the bankruptcy of the social economy, and are there still people who are good at using foreign goods? Naturally, the vast majority of young people are assisting the advancement of domestic product undertakings and moving towards their bright road. However, only a small group of young people are anesthetized by the hateful reality, but temporarily lost their nature and became salesmen for foreign goods, which is not only useless to the future of domestic goods, but also an obstacle to the revival of the social economy.

The fact is this, probably the psychology of this part of the young people is completely anesthetized in the hateful reality, and the invasion of vanity to their hearts, and the pressure of the social environment, naturally, is enough to make them lose their nature. Therefore, wearing suits and leather shoes, (in fact, domestic goods also have leather shoes and suits, but they must not be foreign goods), fully authentic imported goods, go up and down dance halls, wine shops, and even movies must be foreign films. In this way, the rolling outflow of snow-white money every year is not a small number, and the national vitality is also severely depleted several times.

After witnessing these contradictory facts, I think that no matter who it is, they will deeply feel infinite pain, thinking that these people's hearts are dead, but it is useless to be sad. We must have practical methods. Of course, these people have all received higher education, petty bourgeois, or even are still in higher education. Now we naturally only have to promote domestic goods to influence them, but this method still needs to be discussed and decided by us.

Young people are the backbone of society, the masters of our future, the focus of society, and what everyone expects. Moreover, it is also their duty to promote domestic goods. This responsibility and obligation are of course inescapable and cannot be shirked. What's more, in this autumn of turmoil and crisis, how should the young people of our country unite as one and strive to promote domestic goods and block foreign goods, so as to make the country and society's economy the safest and most consolidated way.

Discussion of National Products

Prelude to the National Goods Agency 223

— Duanmu Luzeng

Using domestic goods is of course the bounden duty of the Chinese people: but when needed, many difficulties often arise, such as the difficulty in distinguishing when purchasing, especially those unscrupulous merchants who, for their own benefit, do not hesitate to change the appearance of enemy goods, so that compatriots who love to use domestic goods can easily buy inferior goods if they are not careful. At the same time, there are many compatriots who are unwilling to go to reliable domestic goods stores to purchase because of the distance of their residences, and purchase in nearby stores, so that they mistakenly purchase inferior goods; but there is also a biggest fatal injury that can prevent domestic goods from developing to the society and penetrating into the people, that is, it is difficult for production and consumption to cooperate. On the production side, they often like to cater to the temporary psychology of consumers, so they cannot last; and there are many producers who often like to imitate the products of others that already have considerable value, so that consumers have no choice; and there are many domestic goods who have gained social belief, but because they are unwilling to improve from time to time, the result is still losing social trust; but what about the consumer side? They are unwilling to announce frankly the fine imported products they want, so that domestic goods factories can try to manufacture substitutes; and even if there are domestic goods substitutes, how should they be reformed and researched during use, and the experience after research is also unwilling to be announced to promote the improvement of producers, so that the current domestic goods cannot be improved from time to time; in the meantime, it seems that there is an obstacle between domestic goods and the Chinese people, and they do not communicate with each other and are indifferent, but the real reason is that there is still a lack of a mechanism in China to communicate between domestic goods and the Chinese people; a lack of a spirit to break this obstacle and do practical work.

According to the above situation, it seems to be a pessimistic and serious problem in the domestic goods industry; indeed, this is an extremely pessimistic and extremely serious problem; but recently I have received reliable news that is really worth exciting our spirit, that is, a specialized agency has recently been discovered in Shanghai that solves all the above-mentioned problems! This is a domestic goods agency that works hard and does not advocate empty talk, and specializes in implementing practical work; it is located in the Chinese National Goods Guidance Center attached to the Chinese Vocational Education Society at No. 80 Hualong Road, French Concession, Shanghai. Since September 18th, in view of the increasingly serious national crisis, but saving the country does not advocate empty talk, and if the country wants to be strong, we must first start from promoting domestic goods and guiding producers to strive to improve products; under the cooperation of several famous domestic goods factories in Shanghai and the Chinese Vocational Education Society, the institute was immediately established; since its establishment, the work it has done includes guiding the Chinese people to purchase domestic goods, guiding the production side to strive to improve products, holding exhibitions, investigating the content of domestic goods factories in Shanghai, compiling and printing various books. Recently, it has paid special attention to the cooperation between production and sales, and guiding Russians to purchase domestic goods. However, past experience tells them that if there is no implementing agency, it is impossible to find good results by relying on the power of publicity first, so they resolutely decided to set up a Chinese National Goods Agency, attached to the Chinese National Goods Guidance Center. According to the person in charge of the department, preparations have been made so far, and it has now been officially established to serve domestic people who eat. It handles purchasing affairs on behalf of others. In this city, you only need to notify by telephone, and the department will send someone to contact you. Outside this city, you only need to notify in writing. The method is simple and the cost is saved. It is expected that the future of the department is truly unlimited!

At the same time, the department will conduct a general survey of all agencies, schools, families, and individuals in Shanghai, and report the feelings and improvement opinions of the current domestic goods industry to various domestic goods factories for reference and improvement. At the same time, the department will connect the two lines of production and consumption, so that producers have fine domestic goods products that are especially suitable for the needs of the Chinese people; so that consumers have fine domestic goods products that are especially suitable for their own tastes; at the same time, the department can also prevent the Chinese people from mistakenly purchasing inferior goods, and avoid all kinds of troubles when purchasing goods, and can also get extremely favorable discounts, because every cell of the department is organized by various domestic goods factories in Shanghai; if you, the readers, have any questions, the department will definitely have a very satisfactory answer.

Contributing Opinions

A Suggestion for Domestic Goods Factories 225

— Pillow Wood

Organizing an Exchange for Surplus Materials

Currently, efforts to promote domestic goods are focused on two aspects: advocating the use of domestic goods and manufacturing them. Looking at the establishment of groups promoting domestic goods, the opening of domestic goods companies, and the founding of domestic goods factories, their achievements are evident. However, the development of the domestic goods industry is endless. Our work is truly insignificant and requires even greater effort and expansion. What we must not overlook is finding ways to reduce the cost of raw materials for domestic goods. Only by reducing the cost of raw materials can the price of goods be lowered. Besides increasing the production of raw materials and reducing transportation costs, we should also unite local factories, large and small, to organize an exchange for surplus materials. This exchange could be sponsored by the Association of Machine-Made Domestic Goods Factories. All surplus scraps and waste materials from various factories could be registered and sold through the exchange. Those who need various surplus materials could request representation from the exchange. In this way, factories with excess scrap materials, such as narrow iron strips from canneries, paper scraps from printing houses, rubber scraps from rubber shoe factories, and waste yarn and threads from yarn and cloth factories, can find a renewed purpose and avoid being discarded and wasted. Isn't that ideal? Furthermore, factories that need such raw materials, such as celluloid factories needing rags and wood shavings, and box factories needing paper scraps and cloth edges, can rely on the exchange for supplies, avoiding the trouble of collecting and soliciting, and without fear of running out. Therefore, the organization of an exchange for surplus materials is truly a beneficial measure that achieves two goals with one effort and should not be delayed. May domestic goods manufacturers recognize this and cooperate to contribute to the glory of the domestic goods industry.

A Person of Intention Introduces Several People of Intention 227

— Natural

These past few Sundays, the weather has been very good, so we took advantage of it to go to the interior and rural areas. Changzhou, Wuxi, Caohejing, and Nanxiang were all places we visited. In Changzhou, we saw the Tongcheng Textile Factory and admired Mr. Chi Zongmo's perseverance and enthusiasm in striving for the domestic goods industry. In Wuxi, we saw many tall chimneys and admired the developed entrepreneurial spirit of the people of Wuxi even more. In Caohejing, we saw the Huxi Farm and the agricultural group of the Qianjiao Society, and realized that our vitality lies in such places. Recently, in Nanxiang, we saw Mr. Gu Xiyuan's Revitalization of Rural Subsidiary Occupations Association, which uses the improvement of weaving as a starting point and promotes planting vegetables, raising pigs, sheep, chickens, and fish. After seeing the weaving factory and the plantation, we realized that the words posted on his wall, "No wasted land, no wasted time, no wasted effort, no wasted wealth," were not empty words. His methods of renting and transferring looms are threefold: first, a one-time purchase for 50 yuan per loom; second, an installment purchase, paid in four months, for 55 yuan per loom; third, a rental, paying two yuan per month. If a loom malfunctions, the association will send someone to repair it without charging a repair fee. The money for weaving can be paid to the association at a price (in whole or in part) to collect, or a guarantor can be found for borrowing. The woven cloth must be submitted every five days. The width and length of the cloth are all in accordance with the regulations of the association. Wages are based on the quality of the finished product and the amount of production, with a fixed standard. Mr. Gu pays attention to this kind of work to save the countryside, in addition to his own business. It's admirable and praiseworthy. Later, we visited Mr. Ye Youcai's Shengming Electric Light Factory. He also came with the aim of serving the local area. Not long after taking over, he had two commendable achievements. One is to increase the brightness of the lights, and the other is to reduce electricity bills. He has to sacrifice four to five hundred yuan per month without any reluctance. He is also building a motor factory nearby, which is currently under construction and is very large in scale, giving the people of Xiangdi another place to work. It can be seen that there is no need to worry about the poor and bitter local areas, and the decline of the countryside. What is worrying is that there are only money-hoarders and no entrepreneurs. After a day of traveling in Xiang, the feelings I gained are as follows:

Everyone talks about saving the countryside, but what's the use of empty words? Benefiting others starts with overcoming oneself, and enterprises benefit people more.

Historical Records of Domestic Goods

The Beginning and End of the Nantong Native Cloth Movement 228

— Yu Qiacheng

The sound of cannons on September 18th shook the society of Nantong and Haimen, not only arousing the impulse of national consciousness in the intellectual circles, but also greatly affecting the handicraft weaving industry. Because the bulk cloth of the two counties of Tonghai was sold solely in the Northeast, since the Shenyang Incident, Tonghai cloth had been piling up in Shanghai. Cloth shops were suspended due to stranded funds, and the countryside became increasingly impoverished due to the destruction of subsidiary occupations. The commerce of large and small towns in the two counties of Tonghai suddenly became desolate. This was the objective environment for the formation of the Tonghai Native Cloth Movement.

The initial native cloth movement was also a reform movement. In terms of weaving, new machines and new methods were adopted, which were advocated by public education institutions, and a lot of effort was put into promotion and encouragement. From cities to towns, Tonghai held many native cloth exhibitions and promoted them widely, creating a surging phenomenon for a time.

Because of emotional reasons, under the slogan "Nantong people use Nantong cloth," the improved cloth sold very well, so that all parties purchased machines and manufactured them. There were also many elementary school teachers who put down their teaching whips and went to the looms. However, because production and sales were not controlled, it was not long before, on the one hand, the emotion cooled down and, on the other hand, sales in the countryside were sluggish. In addition, there was competition from the same industry, not in the pursuit of excellence in quality and output, but in reducing materials and lowering prices, so that the reputation of Nantong's improved cloth, before it was replaced to other places, suddenly prospered and then suddenly declined.

The lessons given to us from this Nantong Native Cloth Movement are, on the one hand, the fragility of the foundation of emotional purchasing factors; on the other hand, it is enough to prove that irregular infighting in the same industry is useless. At the same time, the indifference of urban people to rural subsidiary occupations, and the pessimism about the future of national cloth, are also serious problems.

Therefore, this is by no means the responsibility of a few individuals, nor is it a simple problem on one side. If we want to liberate ourselves from the suppression of rayon, we must pay attention to the way out for national cloth, and before the future of the Chinese native cloth movement has been solved for many problems, we must strictly prevent repeating the mistakes of the Nantong reform movement.

Finally, my hope is that the educational and industrial circles of Nantong will work hard again!

Observation Notes

A Visit to Huikang Farm 229

— Lianru

Everyone knows that our country has been an agricultural country since ancient times. The number of farmers accounts for about 88% of the total population of the country, so the bankruptcy of the rural economy is also the bankruptcy of the entire national economy. Recently, aren't we making a fuss about the revitalization of the countryside? Of course, the decline of the rural economy is affected by politics, but we are also too self-defeating and pay too little attention to the subsidiary occupations of farmers. Therefore, not only is the rural economy bankrupt, but also foreign agricultural by-products are constantly being transported to China. In order to promote domestic agricultural by-products to resist foreign goods, and to remedy the rural economy, we must set up more farms to produce more products, such as honey, milk, canned food, etc., and to promote the attention and awareness of farmers.

I have had this idea for a long time and thought about visiting Huikang Farm, but it was not until a few days ago that I was able to fulfill my wish. Although it was early autumn, walking under the morning sun made me sweat a lot. The farm is located at the west end of Sheqiao, Tonghui Road. After a long stretch of coal slag road, we arrived at the farm. More than ten feet away from the south of the farm is a sign with the four large characters "Huikang Farm" written by Mr. Hua Yizhi. The size of the farm is about 20 to 30 acres, surrounded by a very high bamboo fence. After entering the door, the first thing that caught my eye was a very clean and spacious cow farm. There were one or two dozen cows feeding in the farm, and the cows were also very clean. Next to it were the business office and the office. Next door to the east was the milk filling room. A worker in white was working. Milk was released from the milk filling machine, bottle by bottle, without the need for human fingers to touch the milk, which was indeed hygienic. Next door to the east was the bottle washing and disinfection room. The water used for washing bottles was disinfected water and artesian well water. Behind this building was a new-style, light-gathering and ventilated cowshed, which was very high, spacious, and refreshing. The artesian well stood tall on the east side of the house. There were also cold storage rooms and boiler rooms, which I didn't look at carefully one by one, and the valuable space doesn't allow me to write them out carefully one by one.

The founders and managers of this farm are all experts in agricultural affairs, such as Mr. Hua Yizhi, Gao Jianji, Liu Pingjiang, and Huang Xiaomin. The businesses that the farm has already run include sterilized milk, white pagoda oil, honey, and biscuits mixed with milk, honey, and eggs. In order to popularize these by-products, the farm does not hesitate to sacrifice and sell bee breeding, chickens, and dairy cows at low prices. In our country, domestic goods such as white pagoda oil and honey are indeed rare, so it is also worth writing about for fellow citizens who care about domestic goods to see.

Literary Man 丨 A bachelor of arts, who graduated from S University not long ago, with artistic hair, serge suit, white hard collar, Indian silk tie, and leather shoes.

Weaver Girl 丨 A disheveled and strong village girl, wearing a moon-white short cloth jacket, a blue cloth apron, and black cloth shoes.

Literary Man: (Holding a pen, tilting his head, thinking deeply there.)

Weaver Girl: Sir! Can you lend me some black ink to dye the head yarn of the loom?

Literary Man: I only have blue, not black.

Weaver Girl: Sir, don't you use black ink for writing articles?

Literary Man: I use a "Fountain Pen" dipped in "No Stain" to write.

Weaver Girl: What are you saying, sir? I can't understand it.

Literary Man: Hey! Look! (Lifting up his fountain pen.) I always use this pen to write, why would I need black ink!丨. You work so hard weaving cloth, how much money can you earn in a day?

Weaver Girl: To tell you the truth, sir, from early morning to late night, weaving a piece of cloth, the market is not very good, but I can earn half a thousand copper coins. If the market was good a few years ago...

Literary Man: Hey! Half a thousand copper coins, five dimes of silver... I write half a thousand words a day and can earn three or four dollars.

Weaver Girl: (Surprised) Articles! They can't even be exchanged for a piece of tofu at a tofu shop. Can they be sold for money?

Literary Man: As long as the articles are written opportunistically, they are much more promising than weaving cloth.

Weaver Girl: How to be opportunistic?

Literary Man: For example, this year everyone is promoting domestic goods, and factories are spending money to buy publicity articles; as long as you describe the benefits of domestic goods in a flamboyant way, so that every Chinese person should eat domestic products, wear silk cloth, and use domestic goods; promote domestic goods, how it can save the country, how it can force the Japanese dwarfs to death... If you write like this and send it to the newspaper, the editor will nod his head after reading it, and it's guaranteed to be valuable.

Weaver Girl: Oh! So that's how it is. Then why do you, sir, promote domestic goods with all your might, but wear foreign clothes, wear foreign cloth, and write with foreign pens?

Literary Man: Ha! Ha! (Laughing like an egret) I take it for convenience and decency. Moreover... these... China also 丨丨

How to Recognize Domestic Goods? 234

After Disappointment 235

— Shou

In this domestic goods year of reviving national spirit and cultivating national vitality, domestic goods manufacturers are flourishing like bamboo shoots after rain, which is really gratifying. However, in reality, foreign goods still fill the Chinese market and do not shake its solid foundation due to the surge in domestic products. Are the Chinese all blind worshippers of foreign goods? I can't help but feel a little doubtful.

In order to move the place, I specially spent two dollars and some cents to buy a spring lock made by a Chinese. Its style and appearance are really not more "push-back" than imported products. I was very satisfied and installed it on the door and tried my best to promote it to relatives and friends.

But in less than a week, the spring pin installed on the door suddenly broke. After disassembling and examining the details, the reason was very simple; a screw inside the lock was originally broken, but after a short period of use, it came off, and the entire lock was damaged.

This is a very painful thing; I sincerely use domestic goods, but the crudeness and durability of domestic goods are so poor! (Although only a very small number of domestic goods are like this, these black sheep will eventually implicate the reputation of all domestic goods.)

But then again, this error may be mostly due to the laziness and ignorance of the workers. The factory probably wouldn't covet such a small profit and use already broken screws, but it is also unremitting in its dereliction of duty to not inspect the products and rush them to the market for sale. Little has been disappointed and wants to offer a contribution to sincere producers of domestic goods; improve the level of workers, explain the great righteousness, and do not let them neglect their duties (of course, they themselves must never produce crudely and fraudulently), and at the same time, they must strictly inspect the goods, and never allow shoddy products to fill the ranks, losing their reputation. If that is the case, then a ray of dawn for the future of domestic goods is unlimited!
